  >> 4. Flutter Project Architecture (G02)
  >> 4.1 Folder Structure
  >> lib/
  >> ├── core/                         # Shared infrastructure
  >> │   ├── api/                      # Dio client, interceptors, base repo
  >> │   ├── auth/                     # JWT storage, refresh logic
  >> │   ├── cache/                    # Drift DB, Hive boxes
  >> │   ├── config/                   # App config, env vars, feature flags
  >> │   ├── error/                    # Failure classes, error handler
  >> │   ├── localization/             # ARB files, localization delegate
  >> │   ├── network/                  # Connectivity monitor, sync queue
  >> │   ├── router/                   # GoRouter setup, route guards
  >> │   ├── theme/                    # ThemeData, design tokens
  >> ├── features/
  >> │   ├── auth/                     # OTP login + onboarding
  >> │   │   ├── data/                 # AuthRemoteDataSource, AuthLocalDataSource
  >> │   │   ├── domain/               # AuthRepository (abstract), AuthUseCase
  >> │   │   ├── presentation/         # LoginScreen, OtpScreen, OnboardingScreen
  >> │   │   └── providers/            # authProvider, otpTimerProvider
  >> │   ├── farm_os/                  # Farm, Pond, Crop, Feed, Mortality, Water
  >> │   │   ├── data/                 # Remote + Local data sources, DTOs
  >> │   │   ├── domain/               # Farm, Pond, Crop, FeedLog entities + repos
  >> │   │   └── providers/            # farmDashboardProvider, activeCropProvider
  >> │   ├── harvest_marketplace/
  >> │   ├── input_marketplace/
  >> │   ├── advisory/
  >> │   ├── community/
  >> │   ├── chat/
  >> │   ├── notifications/
  >> │   └── profile/
  >> └── main.dart                     # App entrypoint, ProviderScope
  >> 4.2 State Management Patterns
  >> State Type
  >> Solution
  >> Example
  >> Server data (async)
  >> AsyncNotifierProvider (Riverpod 2)
  >> farmDashboardProvider fetches + caches dashboard
  >> Local-only UI state
  >> StateProvider / StateNotifierProvider
  >> Selected pond tab, form field visibility
  >> Realtime updates
  >> StreamProvider wrapping Supabase stream
  >> chatStreamProvider(conversationId)
  >> Offline sync queue
  >> StateNotifierProvider + Drift
  >> pendingSyncProvider — queue of local writes to flush
  >> Auth state
  >> AsyncNotifierProvider with auto-dispose
  >> currentUserProvider — global, no dispose
  >> Feature flags
  >> Provider wrapping Growthbook SDK
  >> featureFlagProvider(flagName) → bool
  >> 4.3 Routing Strategy (GoRouter)
  >> Package
  >> go_router ^13.0
  >> Route Guard
  >> authGuard checks currentUserProvider; redirects to /login if unauthenticated
  >> Role Guard
  >> roleGuard checks user.role; 403 screen for unauthorized routes
  >> Bottom Nav
  >> ShellRoute with 5 branches preserving individual nav stacks
  >> Deep Links
  >> GoRouter handles app:// scheme for push notification payloads
  >> Error Route
  >> /error/:code — catches all unmatched or error routes
  >> 4.4 Offline-First Data Layer
  >> Every feature that requires offline support follows this pattern:
  >> 1. Screen calls UseCase
  >> 2. UseCase calls Repository
  >> 3. Repository first returns Drift (local) data immediately
  >> 4. Repository then fetches from API in background
  >> 5. On success: writes to Drift, emits updated stream
  >> 6. On failure: SyncQueue stores mutation; retries on connectivity
  >> 7. Conflict resolution: server timestamp wins (last-write-wins)
  >> 4.5 Code Standards
  >> Dart version
  >> Dart 3.x — sound null safety, records, patterns required
  >> Linting
  >> flutter_lints + custom analysis_options.yaml (strict)
  >> Naming
  >> snake_case files, PascalCase classes, camelCase variables
  >> Widget size
  >> No widget file exceeds 200 lines; extract to sub-widgets
  >> No BuildContext across async gaps
  >> Always check mounted before using context after await
  >> Error handling
  >> All AsyncNotifier states handle loading/data/error with proper UI
  >> Testing
  >> Each feature must have: 1 widget test + 1 unit test for repository
  >> 5. Payment & Commerce Integration (G03, G18, G23)
  >> 5.1 Razorpay Configuration
  >> Account Type
  >> Razorpay Route (for marketplace payouts to farmers)
  >> Required Products
  >> Subscriptions, Payment Links, Route (Split Payments), Webhooks
  >> Webhook Secret
  >> Stored in AWS Secrets Manager; verified via HMAC-SHA256 signature
  >> Test Mode
  >> All development + staging on Razorpay Test mode; production key via env
  >> Currency
  >> INR only at launch; multi-currency post-Year 1
  >> PCI Compliance
  >> Razorpay handles all card data; platform never touches card numbers
  >> GST on Commission
  >> 18% GST on platform commission amount; GST invoice auto-generated
  >> 5.2 Buyer Subscription Lifecycle
  >> Event
  >> Trigger
  >> System Action
  >> Notification
  >> Trial Start
  >> Buyer clicks 'Start Free Trial'
  >> Create Razorpay subscription (status: trialing); record in subscriptions table
  >> Welcome email + app banner
  >> Trial Ending
  >> 3 days before trial_ends_at
  >> No action — Razorpay auto-charges
  >> Push: 'Trial ending in 3 days — card on file'
  >> First Charge
  >> Razorpay webhook: subscription.charged
  >> Update subscription status → active; unlock tier features
  >> Email: Payment receipt + invoice
  >> Charge Failure
  >> Razorpay webhook: subscription.payment.failed
  >> Downgrade to free tier; set status → past_due
  >> Push + email: 'Payment failed — update card'
  >> Retry Success
  >> Razorpay retry succeeds
  >> Restore tier; set status → active
  >> Email: Payment recovered
  >> Cancellation
  >> Buyer cancels in app
  >> Call Razorpay cancel API; set cancelled_at; maintain access until period_end
  >> Email: Cancellation confirmed
  >> Renewal
  >> Razorpay webhook: subscription.charged (recurring)
  >> Extend current_period_end; log transaction
  >> Email: Renewal receipt
  >> Upgrade
  >> Buyer upgrades plan
  >> Cancel current sub; create new sub; prorate credit
  >> Email: Plan upgraded
  >> 5.3 Harvest Transaction Commission Flow
  >> Step
  >> Actor
  >> Action
  >> System
  >> Farmer
  >> Accepts buyer offer
  >> System: create transaction record (status: pending)
  >> Generate Razorpay Payment Link
  >> Amount = quantity × final_price × 1.015 (1.5% commission)
  >> Send payment link to buyer
  >> Push notification + SMS + in-app message in chat thread
  >> Buyer
  >> Completes payment
  >> Razorpay webhook: payment.captured
  >> Update transaction status → completed
  >> Commission_amount stored; GST invoice generated
  >> Release farmer contact details to buyer
  >> Phone number shared in chat; listing marked as sold
  >> Record commission in analytics
  >> Platform MRR dashboard updated
  >> 5.4 Webhook Endpoint Specification
  >> Webhook Event
  >> Endpoint
  >> Handler Action
  >> payment.captured
  >> POST /webhooks/razorpay
  >> Complete transaction, share farmer contact, send receipts
  >> payment.failed
  >> Mark offer as payment_failed; notify buyer; re-open listing
  >> subscription.charged
  >> Activate/renew subscription tier for user
  >> subscription.payment.failed
  >> Downgrade to free; start dunning email sequence
  >> subscription.cancelled
  >> Set cancellation state; schedule access removal
  >> refund.processed
  >> Update transaction to refunded; restore listing if within 24h
  >> Security Note
  >> 6. Search Architecture — Meilisearch (G05)
  >> 6.1 Index Definitions
  >> Index: harvest_listings
  >> Primary Key
  >> Searchable Attributes
  >> species, district, mandal, farmer_name (display), notes
  >> Filterable Attributes
  >> species, district, size_count, status, is_urgent, harvest_date (unix timestamp)
  >> Sortable Attributes
  >> harvest_date, created_at, quantity_kg, asking_price
  >> Ranking Rules
  >> sort → words → typo → proximity → attribute → exactness
  >> Typo Tolerance
  >> enabled, minWordSizeForTypos: 5
  >> Displayed Attributes
  >> Sync Strategy
  >> PlanetScale webhook → Lambda → Meilisearch update on every INSERT/UPDATE/DELETE
  >> Index: products
  >> name, brand, category, description
  >> category, species_compatibility, crop_stage, supplier_district, is_active, is_featured
  >> offer_price, average_rating, view_count
  >> Synonyms
  >> 'kaduu' → 'feed', 'maatallu' → 'medicine', 'bijam' → 'seed' (Telugu synonyms)
  >> id, name, brand, category, mrp, offer_price, image_url, supplier_name, average_rating
  >> Index: community_posts
  >> body, author_name
  >> species_tag, language, tags, moderation_status
  >> trending_score, created_at, like_count
  >> id, body (truncated 200 chars), author_name, species_tag, like_count, created_at
  >> 6.2 Database → Meilisearch Sync Pipeline
  >> Mechanism
  >> Latency
  >> New harvest listing created
  >> POST /v1/harvest-listings Lambda calls Meilisearch SDK immediately after DB insert
  >> < 500ms
  >> Listing status update
  >> PATCH handler calls Meilisearch update after DB update
  >> Product added/updated
  >> Supplier product Lambda calls Meilisearch update
  >> Community post created/moderated
  >> Post Lambda calls Meilisearch update
  >> Full re-index (recovery)
  >> Scheduled Lambda daily 2 AM — reads DB, rebuilds all indexes
  >> < 5 min
  >> Index health check
  >> UptimeRobot pings GET /health on Meilisearch every 5 min
  >> 7. Chat & Realtime Architecture (G06)
  >> 7.1 Supabase Realtime Channel Strategy
  >> Channel naming
  >> conversation:{conversation_id}
  >> Auth
  >> Supabase RLS policy: only users in conversation.participant_ids can subscribe
  >> Events broadcast
  >> INSERT on messages table auto-broadcast to channel subscribers
  >> Connection management
  >> Flutter app subscribes on chat screen open; unsubscribes on pop
  >> Reconnection
  >> Supabase SDK handles reconnection with exponential backoff automatically
  >> Presence
  >> channel.track({ user_id, is_typing }) for typing indicators
  >> 7.2 Message Types & Metadata Schemas
  >> metadata JSON Structure
  >> Rendered As
  >> text
  >> Plain text bubble
  >> image
  >> { url: string, width: int, height: int, thumbnail_url: string }
  >> Tappable image with lightbox
  >> offer_update
  >> { offer_id, event: 'submitted|accepted|rejected|countered', price, quantity }
  >> Highlighted offer card in chat
  >> system
  >> { event: 'listing_sold|listing_expired|contact_shared', body_te: string, body_en: string }
  >> Grey system message divider
  >> 7.3 Image Sharing in Chat
  >> Detail
  >> User selects image
  >> Flutter image_picker; max 5MB; compressed to 800px, JPEG 80%
  >> Upload to R2
  >> Direct upload via pre-signed URL from POST /v1/chat/media/upload-url
  >> Send message
  >> POST /v1/conversations/{id}/messages with type: image + media_url
  >> Thumbnail generation
  >> Lambda triggered on R2 upload; generates 200px thumbnail; stores as media_url + _thumb
  >> Display
  >> cached_network_image shows thumbnail; full image on tap
  >> 7.4 Read Receipts
  >> Single tick
  >> Message created_at shown — message sent
  >> Double tick (grey)
  >> All participant user_ids are keys in is_read_by — message delivered
  >> Double tick (teal)
  >> All participant user_ids have non-null timestamps in is_read_by — read
  >> PATCH /v1/conversations/{id}/read — marks all messages as read by auth user
  >> 8. KYC & Trust Verification (G07, G20)
  >> 8.1 Farmer KYC Flow
  >> Screen
  >> KYC Intro
  >> Explains benefits of verification; shows document types accepted
  >> Render with benefits list; skip option available
  >> Document Selection
  >> Farmer selects doc type (Aadhaar, PAN, Voter ID)
  >> Guides to appropriate next screen
  >> Document Capture
  >> Camera capture of front + back; or gallery upload
  >> flutter_camera with rectangle overlay; max 5MB; JPEG
  >> Selfie Capture
  >> Selfie with document held next to face
  >> Liveness check guide; send to R2
  >> Upload & Submit
  >> Documents uploaded to R2; kyc_documents record created (status: pending)
  >> POST /v1/kyc/submit; admin notified
  >> Admin Review
  >> Admin reviews in admin panel; checks doc clarity + name match
  >> Approve (user notified) or Reject (reason shown to user)
  >> Outcome
  >> User notified via push + in-app
  >> Approved: badge applied; Rejected: reason + retry option
  >> 8.2 Supplier GSTIN Verification
  >> API Endpoint
  >> GET https://taxpayerapi.gst.gov.in/ext/api/taxpayer/{gstin}
  >> API key from GST developer portal (free for registered taxpayers)
  >> Checks
  >> Business name match (fuzzy), status = Active, registration state = AP
  >> Auto-flag
  >> If name mismatch > 30% Levenshtein distance → flag for manual review
  >> Record
  >> gstin_verified=true + gstin_verified_at stored on supplier approval
  >> Fallback
  >> GST API is often down; admin can manually override with document proof
  >> 8.3 Trust Signals on Platform
  >> Signal
  >> Earned By
  >> Displayed On
  >> Verified Farmer Badge
  >> Completed KYC + 1 completed crop cycle
  >> Harvest listings, community profile
  >> Experienced Farmer Badge
  >> 3+ completed crop cycles on platform
  >> Community posts, profile
  >> Verified Supplier Badge
  >> GSTIN verified + admin approved
  >> Product listings, supplier profile
  >> Trusted Buyer Badge
  >> 3+ completed transactions + no disputes
  >> Offer cards (farmer sees on incoming offer)
  >> Expert Badge
  >> Platform-assigned to qualified advisors
  >> Community posts, advisory responses
  >> Response Rate
  >> Supplier % of inquiries responded to in 48h
  >> Supplier profile
  >> Listing Accuracy Score
  >> Ratio of listings where final sale matches listing description
  >> Hidden; used by algorithm for ranking
  >> 9. Offline Sync & Conflict Resolution (G08)
  >> 9.1 Sync Queue Schema (Local Drift Table)
  >> INTEGER AUTOINCREMENT PK
  >> Local queue entry ID
  >> operation
  >> TEXT (CREATE|UPDATE|DELETE)
  >> CRUD operation type
  >> entity_type
  >> Entity name (feed_log, mortality_log, water_log, crop)
  >> entity_id
  >> TEXT (UUID)
  >> Local UUID of the entity (generated client-side)
  >> payload
  >> TEXT (JSON)
  >> Full serialized entity data
  >> retry_count
  >> INTEGER DEFAULT 0
  >> Number of sync attempts
  >> last_error
  >> TEXT NULLABLE
  >> Last error message for debugging
  >> INTEGER (Unix ms)
  >> Entry timestamp — used for ordering
  >> synced_at
  >> INTEGER NULLABLE
  >> Null until successfully synced
  >> 9.2 Sync Lifecycle
  >> State
  >> Offline write
  >> User performs action while no connectivity
  >> Write to Drift; add to sync_queue; show 'Saved locally' chip
  >> Connectivity restored
  >> ConnectivityMonitor emits connected event
  >> Start SyncWorker; process queue in FIFO order
  >> Sync attempt
  >> SyncWorker dequeues item
  >> POST/PATCH to API with entity payload
  >> Sync success
  >> API returns 200/201
  >> Remove from queue; update local Drift record with server response
  >> Sync failure (4xx)
  >> API returns 400/409
  >> Log error; increment retry_count; if retry_count > 3 → move to dead_letter_queue; notify user
  >> Sync failure (5xx/network)
  >> API unreachable
  >> Exponential backoff: 30s, 2min, 10min, 1h; keep in queue
  >> Conflict (409)
  >> Server rejects due to state mismatch
  >> Apply server-wins policy; update local record with server state; show 'Sync updated' toast
  >> 9.3 Client-Side UUID Generation
  >> 9.4 Data Freshness Indicators
  >> Green sync dot
  >> Data confirmed synced with server within last 10 minutes
  >> Amber cloud icon
  >> Data saved locally; pending sync (connectivity issue)
  >> Red exclamation
  >> Sync failed after 3 retries; user action required
  >> 'Updated X min ago'
  >> Last successful sync timestamp shown on dashboard
  >> 10. DPDP Act Compliance — Data Export & Deletion (G09)
  >> 10.1 Data Export Flow
  >> User Entry Point
  >> Profile → Privacy Settings → 'Download My Data'
  >> Request Processing
  >> Async Lambda job queued; user notified by push when ready (typically < 30 min)
  >> Package Format
  >> ZIP file containing JSON files per data category
  >> Package Contents
  >> Delivery
  >> Secure pre-signed R2 download URL (expires 24h); sent via SMS + push
  >> Retention
  >> Export package deleted from R2 after 24h
  >> Frequency Limit
  >> Maximum 1 export request per 30 days per user
  >> POST /v1/privacy/data-export → 202 Accepted; GET /v1/privacy/data-export/status
  >> 10.2 Account Deletion Flow
  >> Timing
  >> Request
  >> Immediate
  >> User taps 'Delete Account' → confirmation modal with consequences listed
  >> Cooling Off
  >> 0–30 days
  >> Account status = deletion_pending; user can cancel within 30 days; cannot create new content
  >> Pre-deletion notice
  >> Day 27
  >> Push + SMS: 'Your account will be deleted in 3 days. Tap to cancel.'
  >> Hard delete
  >> Day 30
  >> Lambda job executes deletion cascade
  >> Deletion cascade
  >> Confirmation
  >> SMS to original phone: 'Your AquaOS account has been deleted.'
  >> POST /v1/privacy/delete-account → 202 Accepted; DELETE /v1/privacy/delete-account (cancel)
  >> 11. Species-Specific Advisory Rules & Growth Models (G10, G11)
  >> 11.1 Vannamei Shrimp (L. vannamei) — Reference Parameters
  >> Parameter
  >> Optimal Range
  >> Warning Threshold
  >> Critical Threshold
  >> DO (mg/L)
  >> 5.0 – 8.0
  >> < 4.5 or > 9.0
  >> < 3.5
  >> 7.5 – 8.5
  >> < 7.0 or > 8.8
  >> < 6.8 or > 9.2
  >> Temperature (°C)
  >> 23 – 30
  >> < 18 or > 33
  >> < 15 or > 35
  >> Salinity (ppt)
  >> 10 – 30
  >> < 5 or > 35
  >> < 2 or > 40
  >> Ammonia (mg/L)
  >> < 0.1
  >> 0.1 – 0.5
  >> > 0.5
  >> FCR target
  >> 1.4 – 1.8
  >> 1.8 – 2.2
  >> > 2.5
  >> Target survival rate
  >> > 80%
  >> 70 – 80%
  >> < 60%
  >> Mortality threshold
  >> < 0.1%/day
  >> 0.1 – 0.5%/day
  >> > 0.5%/day
  >> 11.2 Vannamei Growth Curve Model
  >> Growth Equation
  >> W(t) = 0.00001 × L(t)^3.05 where L(t) = L∞ × (1 - e^(-K(t-t0)))
  >> Parameters (AP calibration)
  >> L∞ = 195mm, K = 0.025/day, t0 = -20 days
  >> Expected size at Day 90
  >> ~18–20g (50–55 count/kg)
  >> Expected size at Day 120
  >> ~25–28g (35–40 count/kg)
  >> Survival correction
  >> Weight estimate × (current estimated survival % / 100)
  >> Display on dashboard
  >> 'Est. size: ~30 count (Day 95)' + '±15% estimate' disclaimer
  >> Recalibration
  >> Model will be updated quarterly using actual transaction data from platform
  >> 11.3 Tiger Prawn Reference Parameters
  >> Warning
  >> Critical
  >> 4.5 – 7.0
  >> < 4.0
  >> < 3.0
  >> < 7.2 or > 9.0
  >> < 7.0
  >> 15 – 25
  >> < 10 or > 30
  >> 1.5 – 2.0
  >> 2.0 – 2.5
  >> > 2.8
  >> Stocking density
  >> 6 – 10 PL/sqm
  >> 10 – 15 PL/sqm
  >> > 15 PL/sqm
  >> 11.4 Fish (Rohu/Catla) Reference Parameters
  >> 5.0 – 9.0
  >> 7.0 – 8.5
  >> < 6.5 or > 9.5
  >> < 6.0
  >> 25 – 32
  >> < 10
  >> 1.8 – 2.5
  >> 2.5 – 3.0
  >> > 3.5
  >> 3,000–5,000 fingerlings/acre
  >> 5,000–8,000/acre
  >> > 10,000/acre

  >> 12.2 Content Production Checklist
  >> Draft all 40 messages in Telugu first; English translation second
  >> Expert review by AP State Fisheries Department officer or academic
  >> Farmer readability test: 5 farmers of varying literacy levels
  >> Regional dialect check: Godavari Telugu vs Nellore Telugu vocabulary differences
  >> Length validation: title ≤ 50 chars Telugu; body ≤ 250 chars Telugu (fits push notification)
  >> Message must include: 1 specific observation, 1 specific action, 1 expected outcome
  >> 13. Pricing Intelligence Architecture (G13)
  >> 13.1 Data Source Strategy
  >> Source
  >> Data Available
  >> Frequency
  >> Method
  >> Phase
  >> Nellore Shrimp Market Reports
  >> Spot prices for vannamei by count, daily
  >> Daily 8 AM
  >> Puppeteer Lambda scraper → parse HTML → store
  >> Phase 1
  >> MPEDA Weekly Reports
  >> Export prices by species/grade
  >> Weekly
  >> PDF extraction Lambda via pdf-parse
  >> NCS (National Cold Storage) boards
  >> Farm gate prices Bhimavaram
  >> 3× weekly
  >> Scraper + fallback: manual entry by field agent
  >> Kakinada Fish Market
  >> Fish species daily prices
  >> Daily
  >> WhatsApp API: field agent sends photo → OCR Lambda
  >> Phase 2
  >> Platform transactions (derived)
  >> Actual farm-gate prices from accepted offers
  >> Real-time
  >> Analytics event on offer.accepted → price store
  >> Phase 1 (partial)
  >> Supplier product prices
  >> Input cost trends (feed, medicine)
  >> On update
  >> Product listing update event
  >> 13.2 Scraper Lambda Architecture
  >> Runtime
  >> Node.js Lambda with Puppeteer (headless Chrome via chromium-lambda layer)
  >> Schedule
  >> AWS EventBridge rule: 0 8 * * * (8 AM IST daily)
  >> If scrape fails: use yesterday's price + add (stale) flag; alert admin
  >> Anti-scraping
  >> Randomised user-agent, 5–15s delays between requests, max 3 retries
  >> Data validation
  >> Price sanity check: reject if > 50% change from 7-day moving average
  >> Manual override
  >> Admin panel allows manual price entry to correct scrape errors
  >> Storage
  >> daily_prices table + Upstash Redis cache (1h TTL for /pricing/daily endpoint)
  >> 13.3 Price Alert Configuration
  >> Alert trigger
  >> Price change > 10% from previous day for a species + size combination
  >> Farmer targeting
  >> Alert sent to farmers with active crops of that species
  >> Buyer targeting
  >> Alert sent to buyers with saved searches matching that species/district
  >> Channel
  >> Push notification (opted-in users) + in-app price banner
  >> 8:30 AM daily if prices have been updated; never sent without fresh data
  >> 14. Referral Program Mechanics (G14)
  >> 14.1 Referral Flow
  >> Farmer A
  >> Taps 'Invite Friends' in Profile
  >> Display referral_code + pre-filled WhatsApp share message in Telugu
  >> Farmer B
  >> Receives WhatsApp message; downloads app
  >> Play Store link includes referral_code as UTM parameter
  >> Enters referral code at registration (or auto-detected from UTM)
  >> System validates code; creates referrals record (status: pending)
  >> Creates first crop cycle
  >> System checks: qualification_event = first_crop; status → qualified
  >> Reward distributed
  >> Farmer A: 30-day premium advisory unlock; Farmer B: 30-day premium advisory unlock
  >> Referral chain limited
  >> Max 3 reward levels deep; no pyramid scheme; no cash rewards at launch
  >> 14.2 Referral Rewards (Phase 1)
  >> Referrer reward
  >> 30-day 'Advisory Pro' unlock (premium alert frequency + advisor chat)
  >> Referred reward
  >> 30-day 'Advisory Pro' unlock
  >> Maximum rewards per user
  >> 20 referrals (20 months of Advisory Pro) — capped to prevent gaming
  >> Reward delivery
  >> Automatic on qualification event; push notification to both parties
  >> Cash rewards
  >> Not at Phase 1 — Phase 2 consideration pending economics review
  >> 14.3 Referral Analytics
  >> Farmer's referral dashboard
  >> Shows: code, total referred, qualified count, rewards earned
  >> Admin view
  >> Referral network graph; top referrers; suspicious patterns (same IP, bulk)
  >> Fraud prevention
  >> Same device registrations via referral: 24h cooling period before qualifying
  >> 15. Community Post Ranking Algorithm (G16)
  >> 15.1 Trending Score Formula
  >> trending_score = (likes × 2 + comments × 3 + shares × 5 + views × 0.1) / (hours_since_post + 2)^1.5
  >> Likes weight
  >> 2 — basic engagement signal
  >> Comments weight
  >> 3 — stronger signal; conversation = quality content
  >> Shares weight
  >> 5 — strongest signal; WhatsApp share = high trust recommendation
  >> Views weight
  >> 0.1 — weak signal; reduces gaming by view inflation
  >> Time decay exponent
  >> 1.5 — moderate decay; older posts fall off without new engagement
  >> Pinned posts
  >> Pinned posts always appear first regardless of score; max 3 pinned
  >> New post boost
  >> Posts < 2 hours old get trending_score × 1.5 multiplier for discovery
  >> 15.2 Feed Curation Logic
  >> Default feed sort
  >> Trending score descending (community tab)
  >> Species filter
  >> Filter by farmer's active crop species (personalisation)
  >> District filter
  >> Boost posts from same district × 1.3 score multiplier
  >> Language filter
  >> Telugu-first; mixed feed allowed; no English-only posts appear by default
  >> Verified boost
  >> Posts from Verified/Experienced farmers × 1.2 multiplier
  >> Report penalty
  >> Each report reduces score by 15% (max -50% from reports; full hide at 5 reports)
  >> Recalculation frequency
  >> Every 30 minutes (Lambda cron); immediate recalc on new comment/like
  >> 16. Image Moderation Pipeline (G17)
  >> 16.1 Upload → Moderation → Display Flow
  >> Where
  >> Client
  >> Flutter compresses image: max 1200px long edge, JPEG 85%, max 2MB
  >> < 1s device
  >> POST /v1/media/upload-url returns pre-signed R2 PUT URL (60s expiry)
  >> < 200ms
  >> Client PUTs image directly to R2 (bypasses API servers — cost saving)
  >> < 3s on 4G
  >> R2 triggers webhook to Lambda on object creation
  >> Lambda
  >> AWS Rekognition DetectModerationLabels called on image
  >> < 1.5s
  >> Image metadata stored: { url, status: approved|pending|quarantined, width, height }
  >> < 100ms
  >> Client polls GET /v1/media/{id}/status; shows spinner until approved
  >> Typically < 5s total
  >> Approved images displayed; quarantined images replaced with placeholder
  >> 16.2 Rekognition Configuration
  >> AWS Rekognition: DetectModerationLabels
  >> MinConfidence
  >> 40% — flag for review; 70% — auto-quarantine
  >> Categories blocked
  >> Explicit Nudity, Violence, Visually Disturbing, Gambling (all auto-quarantine)
  >> Cost
  >> $0.001 per image; free tier: 5,000 images/month
  >> If Rekognition unavailable: images set to pending_review; admin reviews manually
  >> Admin review queue
  >> Admin panel shows all pending_review images with approve/reject action
  >> Harvest listing photos
  >> Lower risk; only Explicit Nudity auto-quarantined; others flagged for review
  >> 17. Dispute Resolution Workflow (G19)
  >> 17.1 Dispute Initiation
  >> Timeline
  >> Buyer or Farmer
  >> Taps 'Report Issue' on completed transaction
  >> Within 7 days of completion
  >> Platform
  >> Transaction status → in_dispute; both parties notified
  >> Complainant
  >> Submits: issue category, description (max 500 chars), up to 5 photos as evidence
  >> Within 24h of raising dispute
  >> Respondent
  >> Receives notification; can submit counter-evidence: description + photos
  >> Within 48h of complaint
  >> Platform (auto)
  >> Chat transcript from negotiation thread attached automatically as evidence
  >> Admin
  >> Reviews evidence in admin dispute panel; makes resolution decision
  >> Within 5 business days (SLA)
  >> Resolution
  >> Admin selects: Full refund / Partial refund (% specified) / No action + reason
  >> Within 5 business days
  >> Execution
  >> If refund: Razorpay refund API triggered; if no refund: decision communicated
  >> Within 2 business days of resolution
  >> Appeal
  >> Both parties have 3 days to appeal; one appeal per dispute allowed
  >> Within 3 days of resolution
  >> 17.2 Dispute Categories
  >> Quality Mismatch
  >> Harvested shrimp size/quality differs significantly from listing
  >> Quantity Shortage
  >> Actual quantity delivered less than agreed
  >> No Show
  >> Farmer unavailable at agreed harvest date
  >> Payment Not Received
  >> Farmer claims payment not received (despite platform record)
  >> Specimen Issue
  >> Diseased or dead shrimp delivered
  >> Communication Breakdown
  >> Buyer/farmer unresponsive after offer acceptance
  >> 17.3 Dispute Prevention Design
  >> Harvest listings require photos — visual baseline reduces 'quality mismatch' disputes
  >> In-app chat is the record — all negotiation terms visible and timestamped
  >> Payment via platform (not cash) creates payment proof eliminating payment disputes
  >> Verified farmer badge requires crop cycle data — reduces fake listing risk

  >> 18.4 Performance Test Specification (k6)
  >> Smoke test
  >> 10 virtual users, 1 minute — basic sanity
  >> Load test
  >> 500 VU ramp 0→500 over 5 min, hold 10 min — normal load
  >> Stress test
  >> 1,000 VU ramp over 10 min — find breaking point
  >> Spike test
  >> Instant 2,000 VU for 1 min — simulate viral moment
  >> Soak test
  >> 200 VU for 2 hours — memory leaks and connection pool exhaustion
  >> Acceptance criteria
  >> p95 response < 800ms at 500 VU; error rate < 0.1%
  >> 19. Deep Links & App Store Strategy (G21, G28)
  >> 19.1 Deep Link Architecture
  >> Route
  >> URL Scheme
  >> Behaviour
  >> Harvest listing detail
  >> aquaos://listings/{id}
  >> WhatsApp share, buyer notification
  >> Opens listing; if not installed → Play Store → app → listing
  >> Farm dashboard
  >> aquaos://farm/dashboard
  >> Dashboard push notification
  >> Opens farm dashboard
  >> Advisory alert
  >> aquaos://advisory/{alert_id}
  >> Advisory push notification

  >> 21. Disaster Recovery & Security Testing (G24, G47)
  >> 21.1 Disaster Recovery Targets
  >> Scenario
  >> Recovery Procedure
  >> Lambda service disruption
  >> AWS auto-heals Lambda; API Gateway returns 503 during outage; retry at client
  >> PlanetScale primary failure
  >> < 2 min
  >> < 30 sec
  >> PlanetScale auto-failover to read replica; client retries 3× before error screen
  >> Cloudflare R2 outage
  >> < 30 min
  >> Images display cached versions; uploads queued locally; manual review post-recovery
  >> Supabase Auth outage
  >> < 10 min
  >> Existing JWT tokens remain valid (15 min TTL); no new logins until recovery; banner shown
  >> Complete AWS region failure
  >> < 4 hours
  >> < 1 hour
  >> Redeploy CDK stack to ap-south-1 (Mumbai backup region); DNS failover via Cloudflare
  >> Data corruption event
  >> < 8 hours
  >> < 24 hours
  >> Restore PlanetScale to last backup (daily automated); replay CloudWatch logs
  >> Security breach
  >> < 2 hours (contain)
  >> Rotate all secrets; revoke all JWTs; notify affected users; 72h CERT-In report
  >> 21.2 Backup Strategy
  >> PlanetScale automated backup
  >> Daily at 2 AM IST; retained 7 days (free tier) / 30 days (Pro)
  >> R2 object versioning
  >> Enabled on media bucket; 30-day version retention
  >> Infrastructure (CDK)
  >> Git repository is the backup; re-deploy from code at any time
  >> Secrets
  >> AWS Secrets Manager stores all secrets; access audit logged
  >> Export to S3
  >> Weekly Lambda exports full DB to encrypted S3 Glacier for long-term retention

  >> 22. API Error Codes & Rate Limits (G25, G26)
  >> 22.1 Error Response Format
  >> 22.2 Error Code Registry
  >> Code
  >> HTTP Status
  >> Client Action
  >> AUTH_INVALID_TOKEN
  >> JWT expired or malformed
  >> Refresh token; if fails, re-login
  >> AUTH_INSUFFICIENT_ROLE
  >> Role does not have permission for this resource
  >> Show 'Access denied' screen
  >> OTP_INVALID
  >> OTP does not match or expired
  >> Show error; allow resend after 60s
  >> OTP_RATE_LIMIT
  >> Too many OTP requests for this phone
  >> Show cooldown timer
  >> FARM_NOT_FOUND
  >> Farm ID does not exist or not owned by user
  >> Navigate back; show toast
  >> POND_ACTIVE_CROP
  >> Cannot delete pond with active crop
  >> Prompt: harvest or abandon crop first
  >> CROP_ALREADY_ACTIVE
  >> Pond already has an active crop
  >> Show current active crop; offer to view
  >> LISTING_EXPIRED
  >> Harvest listing has expired
  >> Prompt: create new listing
  >> OFFER_ALREADY_ACCEPTED
  >> Another offer on listing was accepted
  >> Show listing closed screen
  >> OFFER_EXPIRED
  >> Offer exceeded 24h window
  >> Notify: offer expired; create new
  >> SUPPLIER_NOT_VERIFIED
  >> Supplier profile pending admin approval
  >> Show verification pending screen
  >> SUBSCRIPTION_REQUIRED
  >> Feature requires active subscription
  >> Show subscription upgrade screen
  >> RATE_LIMIT_EXCEEDED
  >> Too many requests
  >> Retry-After header; exponential backoff
  >> MEDIA_TOO_LARGE
  >> Upload exceeds 5MB limit
  >> Client should compress before retry
  >> MEDIA_TYPE_INVALID
  >> Unsupported file type (not JPEG/PNG)
  >> Show supported formats
  >> VALIDATION_ERROR
  >> Request body fails schema validation
  >> field property identifies invalid field
  >> DUPLICATE_SUBMISSION
  >> Idempotency-Key already processed
  >> Return original response from cache
  >> INTERNAL_ERROR
  >> Unexpected server error
  >> Show generic error; log to Sentry
  >> SERVICE_UNAVAILABLE
  >> Downstream service (DB/cache) unavailable
  >> Retry after 30s; check status page

  >> 23.1 Accessibility Requirements
  >> Requirement
  >> Standard
  >> Implementation
  >> Screen reader support
  >> WCAG 2.1 AA
  >> All interactive elements have Semantics() wrappers with meaningful labels in Telugu
  >> Colour contrast
  >> WCAG AA (4.5:1 normal text, 3:1 large)
  >> Design tokens verified via Colour Contrast Analyser
  >> Touch target size
  >> WCAG 2.5.5 (48×48dp)
  >> All buttons, chips, list items ≥ 48×48dp
  >> Text scaling
  >> Support 50%–200% system font scale
  >> Use sp units; test at 200% scale on Samsung A14
  >> Error identification
  >> WCAG 3.3.1
  >> All form errors identified in text (not colour alone)
  >> Focus indicators
  >> WCAG 2.4.7
  >> Custom FocusDecoration on all focusable widgets
  >> TalkBack compatibility
  >> Android TalkBack
  >> Test all P0 journeys with TalkBack enabled
  >> 23.2 Low-End Device Optimisation
  >> Optimisation
  >> Impact
  >> Image lazy loading
  >> cached_network_image with memCacheWidth 400px
  >> −60% memory on image-heavy screens
  >> List virtualisation
  >> ListView.builder (never ListView with children array)
  >> Smooth scroll on 2GB RAM devices
  >> Animation reduction
  >> MediaQuery.reduceMotion check; disable parallax/complex animations
  >> Prevents jank on GPU-constrained devices
  >> APK split by ABI
  >> flutter build apk --split-per-abi
  >> arm64-v8a APK ≈ 15MB vs 30MB universal
  >> Image precompilation
  >> flutter build with --no-shrink; deferred loading for feature modules
  >> Faster cold start
  >> Local DB pagination
  >> Drift queries with LIMIT/OFFSET; never load all rows
  >> Prevents OOM on 2GB devices
  >> Background task budget
  >> WorkManager battery-aware scheduling; avoid wake locks
  >> Preserves battery on budget phones
  >> Network timeout
  >> Dio timeout: 15s connect, 30s receive; cancel on screen exit
  >> Prevents hanging on 2G edge cases
  >> 23.3 Dark Mode
  >> Support
  >> Optional — Phase 2 feature; Phase 1 light mode only
  >> Design Tokens
  >> System follow
  >> When implemented: ThemeMode.system respects device dark mode setting
  >> Override

  >> 25. BNPL, Webhooks & GST Invoices (G38, G39, G45)
  >> 25.1 Enterprise Buyer Webhook System
  >> Webhook Events
  >> new_listing_matched (saved search match), offer_accepted, listing_expired
  >> Registration
  >> Enterprise buyers register webhook URL + secret in Buyer Dashboard settings
  >> HTTPS POST with JSON payload + HMAC-SHA256 signature header
  >> Retry
  >> 3 retries with 5 min, 30 min, 2h intervals on non-2xx response
  >> Payload Format
  >> { event, timestamp, data: { listing | offer | transaction } }
  >> Verification
  >> Same signature pattern as Razorpay webhook; buyer verifies with their registered secret
  >> Dead letter
  >> Failed webhooks after 3 retries logged; buyer notified via email
  >> 25.2 GST Invoice Generation for Platform Commission
  >> Details
  >> Transaction completed
  >> System records commission_amount + buyer details
  >> Invoice generation
  >> Lambda generates GST-compliant invoice as PDF
  >> Invoice fields
  >> PDF uploaded to R2 at invoices/{year}/{month}/{invoice_number}.pdf
  >> Link sent to buyer via email; downloadable from buyer dashboard
  >> Monthly statement
  >> Batch invoice PDF with all monthly transactions; auto-emailed on 1st of month
  >> 25.3 BNPL (Buy Now Pay at Harvest) — Architecture Outline
  >> NBFC Partner
  >> Avanti Finance or Samunnati (aquaculture-focused NBFCs)
  >> Eligibility
  >> Farmer has 1+ completed crop cycles on platform + KYC verified
  >> Credit Assessment
  >> Loan Flow
  >> Repayment
  >> At harvest: platform deducts loan amount from harvest proceeds before releasing to farmer
  >> Platform role
  >> Loan servicer (not lender); NBFC carries credit risk; platform earns referral fee

  >> Serviceable Obtainable Market Y1
  >> ₹120 Crore GMV (0.2% market capture)
  >> Farmers in AP (addressable)
  >> ~2.5 lakh aquaculture farmer families
  >> Buyers (exporters + processors)
  >> 3,500+ registered in AP
  >> Input Suppliers
  >> 800+ registered dealers in AP
  >> Platform Revenue Target Y1
  >> ₹1.2 Crore (commissions + subscriptions)
  >> Platform Revenue Target Y3
  >> ₹28 Crore (full ecosystem monetisation)

  >> Hardware dependent, not in India
  >> Software-only, zero upfront cost

  >> Crop farming, not aquaculture

  >> Full ecosystem OS

  >> 5. Module Specifications
  >> 5.1 Farm OS Module
  >> 5.1.1 Farm Creation & Management
  >> Screen
  >> Farm Setup Wizard (3-step onboarding)
  >> Step 1
  >> Farm name, district, mandal, village
  >> Step 2
  >> Total acres, water source, GPS (auto or manual)
  >> Step 3
  >> Privacy settings (location visibility)
  >> POST /v1/farms — returns farm ID + dashboard activation
  >> Validation
  >> District must be valid AP district; area between 0.1–5000 acres
  >> Offline
  >> Form data cached locally, synced on connectivity restore
  >> 5.1.2 Pond Management
  >> Pond Manager (grid view + individual pond cards)
  >> Pond Card Shows
  >> Name, area, current crop species, crop age (days), health status
  >> Add Pond Flow
  >> Name → area → depth → aerator count → shape → save
  >> Visual
  >> Color-coded status: Green (healthy), Amber (advisory alert), Red (critical)
  >> POST /v1/farms/{id}/ponds, GET /v1/farms/{id}/ponds
  >> Max Ponds
  >> 100 per farm (soft limit, configurable by admin)
  >> 5.1.3 Crop Cycle Management
  >> Start Crop Flow
  >> Species → stocking date → seed count → seed source → target size
  >> Auto-Calculations
  >> Seed density (count/sqm), expected harvest date, crop age (days)
  >> Dashboard Triggers
  >> Crop creation activates: daily feed reminders, advisory monitoring, survival tracking
  >> Supported Species
  >> Whiteleg Shrimp (L. vannamei), Tiger Prawn, Rohu, Catla, Crab, Others
  >> POST /v1/ponds/{id}/crops, GET /v1/ponds/{id}/crops/active
  >> 5.1.4 Feed Logging
  >> Feed Log Entry (daily tap-and-go interface)
  >> Fields
  >> Feed brand (autocomplete from product catalog), quantity (kg), stage (morning/afternoon/evening)
  >> Smart Defaults
  >> Last-used brand pre-filled; quantity suggestion based on FCR model
  >> Reminder
  >> Daily push notification at 7 AM if feed not logged
  >> Running Total
  >> Cumulative feed displayed on pond card (auto-updates FCR)
  >> POST /v1/crops/{id}/feed-logs, GET /v1/crops/{id}/feed-logs
  >> 5.1.5 Mortality Logging
  >> Mortality Log Entry (quick-entry with symptom checklist)
  >> Date, count, observed symptoms (multi-select), notes
  >> Symptom Library
  >> 20+ pre-defined symptoms (white spot, black gill, EMS, etc.)
  >> Alert Trigger
  >> Mortality > 0.5% of stock/day → immediate advisory alert
  >> Updates estimated survival rate on crop dashboard
  >> POST /v1/crops/{id}/mortality-logs
  >> 5.1.6 Water Quality Logging
  >> Parameters
  >> DO (mg/L), pH, salinity (ppt), temperature (°C), turbidity, ammonia
  >> Entry Method
  >> Manual entry or future IoT sensor auto-sync
  >> Alert Thresholds
  >> DO < 4 mg/L → critical alert; pH < 7 or > 8.5 → warning
  >> POST /v1/crops/{id}/water-logs
  >> 5.1.7 Farm Dashboard
  >> Active Ponds
  >> Card-based layout, one card per active crop
  >> Each Card Shows
  >> Pond name, species, crop age, estimated survival %, FCR, feed today (Y/N)
  >> Summary Strip
  >> Total active ponds | Total estimated harvest (kg) | Advisory alerts count
  >> Quick Actions
  >> Log Feed, Log Mortality, View Advisory, List Harvest
  >> Refresh
  >> Pull-to-refresh; auto-refresh every 10 min in background
  >> Cache Strategy
  >> Dashboard response cached in Redis 5 min TTL, invalidated on any write
  >> GET /v1/farmer/dashboard — aggregated response, single API call
  >> 5.2 Advisory Engine
  >> 5.2.1 Advisory Input Sources
  >> Crop Data
  >> Age, species, stocking density, FCR, mortality rate (from Crop Service)
  >> Feed Data
  >> Daily consumption vs. target, missed feed days (from Feed Logs)
  >> Water Quality
  >> DO, pH, salinity, temperature (from Water Logs or IoT)
  >> Weather Data
  >> Open-Meteo API: temperature, rainfall, wind speed, humidity forecast
  >> Disease Reports
  >> Community-reported outbreaks in same district (from Community Service)
  >> Mortality Patterns
  >> Mortality rate acceleration over 72-hour rolling window
  >> 5.2.2 Advisory Rule Library
  >> Rule Name
  >> Trigger Condition
  >> Severity
  >> Recommended Action
  >> Feed Overuse Alert
  >> FCR > 2.2 for 3 consecutive days
  >> MEDIUM
  >> Reduce feed by 20%, check DO levels
  >> Missed Feed Alert
  >> No feed log for 24h on active crop
  >> Log feed; check pond accessibility
  >> Mortality Spike
  >> Mortality > 0.5% stock/24h
  >> HIGH
  >> Collect samples, contact advisor
  >> Low DO Warning
  >> DO < 4.5 mg/L logged
  >> Increase aeration immediately
  >> pH Imbalance
  >> pH < 7.0 or > 8.8
  >> Apply lime or organic acid
  >> Disease Nearby
  >> Outbreak reported within 30km
  >> Increase monitoring frequency
  >> Storm Warning
  >> Rain > 50mm/24h forecast
  >> Reduce feed, check pond bunds
  >> Heat Stress
  >> Water temp > 33°C logged or forecast
  >> Reduce feeding, increase aeration
  >> Harvest Window
  >> Crop age > 90 days + size estimate meets target
  >> INFO
  >> Consider harvest, check market prices
  >> Low Survival Projection
  >> Estimated survival < 60%
  >> Emergency advisor consultation
  >> FCR Improving
  >> FCR decreasing for 5 days
  >> Good performance — maintain regime
  >> Weight Milestone
  >> Estimated size crosses key count threshold
  >> Sample size, update listing estimate
  >> 5.2.3 Advisory Delivery
  >> Immediate delivery for HIGH severity alerts
  >> In-App Banner
  >> Persistent until acknowledged for MEDIUM+ alerts
  >> SMS Fallback
  >> Sent if push notification not delivered within 10 min (HIGH only)
  >> Language
  >> Telugu default; English optional; Hindi future
  >> Advisory History
  >> All alerts stored 12 months; accessible from farm dashboard
  >> Snooze
  >> Farmer can snooze MEDIUM alerts 24h; HIGH alerts cannot be snoozed
  >> 5.3 Harvest Marketplace
  >> 5.3.1 Harvest Listing Creation
  >> Create Listing (4 fields, 2 taps to publish)
  >> Species
  >> Auto-populated from active crop (editable)
  >> Size/Count
  >> Count per kg (e.g. 30, 40, 50, 60, 70, 80) — dropdown
  >> Quantity
  >> Kg available (minimum 50 kg)
  >> Harvest Date
  >> Calendar picker (today or future, max 14 days)
  >> Asking Price
  >> Optional; market price shown as reference
  >> Photos
  >> Upload up to 5 pond/shrimp photos (compressed to 800px, stored in R2)
  >> Urgent Flag
  >> Toggle — surfaces listing higher in buyer search
  >> Expiry
  >> Auto-expires in 72 hours; farmer notified 12h before expiry
  >> Auto-populated from farm; visible to buyers
  >> POST /v1/harvest-listings — returns listing ID + WhatsApp share link
  >> 5.3.2 Buyer Discovery & Search
  >> Search Filters
  >> Species, district, size count range, harvest date range, quantity
  >> Sort Options
  >> Newest, harvest date, quantity (high/low), price (if provided)
  >> Listing Card
  >> Species, size, quantity, location (district), harvest date, asking price (if set)
  >> Map View
  >> District-level clusters (not exact farm location unless farmer opted in)
  >> Saved Searches
  >> Buyers save filter presets; notified when matching listings appear
  >> Verified Badge
  >> Listings from verified farmers (completed 2+ crop cycles) get a badge
  >> GET /v1/harvest-listings?species=&district=&date_from=&date_to=&size_min=&size_max=
  >> 5.3.3 Offer & Negotiation System
  >> Offer Submission
  >> Buyer enters price per kg + quantity + notes → sends to farmer
  >> Farmer Actions
  >> Accept, Reject, Counter-offer
  >> Counter Flow
  >> Farmer enters counter-price → buyer gets notification → same flow
  >> Chat Integration
  >> Each offer automatically opens a conversation thread in Chat Service
  >> Offer Expiry
  >> Buyer offer expires in 24 hours if no farmer response
  >> Status Tracking
  >> Both parties see offer status in real-time via Supabase Realtime
  >> Transaction Record
  >> Accepted offer logged as transaction in Payment Service
  >> Commission
  >> Platform charges 1.5% of transaction value (collected from buyer)
  >> POST /v1/harvest-listings/{id}/offers, PATCH /v1/offers/{id}
  >> 5.4 Input Marketplace
  >> 5.4.1 Product Categories
  >> Feed
  >> Branded pellet feed by stage (starter, grower, finisher) + species
  >> Seed / Post-larvae
  >> Certified PLs from registered hatcheries
  >> Medicines & Chemicals
  >> Antibiotics, probiotics, disinfectants (licensed suppliers only)
  >> Probiotics
  >> Water and gut probiotics by brand
  >> Aerators
  >> Paddle wheel, propeller types by horsepower
  >> Equipment
  >> DO meters, pH meters, nets, sampling equipment
  >> Pond Prep Chemicals
  >> Lime, dolomite, fertilizers
  >> 5.4.2 Supplier Onboarding
  >> Business name, GSTIN, license type, district coverage
  >> Verification
  >> Admin manually verifies GSTIN and license within 48 hours
  >> Product Listing
  >> Supplier adds products with: name, brand, category, unit, MRP, offer price, minimum order
  >> Subscription
  >> ₹6,000–₹15,000/month depending on listing count and featured placement
  >> Analytics Access
  >> Supplier sees: views, inquiries, conversion rates, district demand heatmap
  >> POST /v1/suppliers, POST /v1/products, GET /v1/products?category=&district=
  >> 5.4.3 Farmer Procurement Flow
  >> Discovery
  >> Browse by category → filter by brand, district, price → product detail
  >> Inquiry
  >> Tap 'Get Quote' → fills quantity → message sent to supplier
  >> Lead Routing
  >> Supplier receives push notification + email with farmer contact
  >> Order Tracking
  >> Basic order status (confirmed, dispatched, delivered) via manual supplier update
  >> Reviews
  >> Post-delivery, farmer rates supplier 1–5 stars with optional comment
  >> Price Intelligence
  >> MRP displayed; offer price shown; historical lowest price shown
  >> 5.5 Farmer Community
  >> Post Types
  >> Text post, photo post, question post, poll
  >> Tags
  >> Species, topic (feed, disease, harvest, general)
  >> Telugu primary, Hindi, English supported
  >> Image Upload
  >> Up to 4 images per post (compressed, R2 stored)
  >> Engagement
  >> Like, comment, share (WhatsApp share), save post
  >> Verification Badge
  >> Farmers with 3+ completed crop cycles get 'Experienced' badge
  >> Advisor Badge
  >> Platform-verified advisors get 'Expert' badge
  >> Trending
  >> Algorithm based on engagement rate within 48h
  >> Moderation
  >> Admin flags + community reports → admin review queue
  >> Abuse Detection
  >> Keyword filter + report system; 3 reports → auto-suspend pending review
  >> POST /v1/posts, GET /v1/posts?tag=&sort=trending, POST /v1/posts/{id}/comments
  >> 6. Complete API Specification
  >> 6.1 API Design Principles
  >> Base URL
  >> https://api.aquaos.in/v1
  >> Protocol
  >> HTTPS only (TLS 1.3 minimum)
  >> Format
  >> JSON request and response bodies
  >> Bearer JWT in Authorization header for all private endpoints
  >> Versioning
  >> URL path versioning (/v1, /v2); old versions supported 12 months
  >> Rate Limiting
  >> 100 req/min per user (public), 500 req/min (buyer/supplier)
  >> Pagination
  >> Cursor-based for lists: ?cursor=&limit=20 (max 100)
  >> Error Format
  >> { error: { code, message, field?, details? } }
  >> HTTP Status
  >> 200 OK, 201 Created, 400 Bad Request, 401 Unauth, 403 Forbidden, 404, 429, 500
  >> Idempotency
  >> POST requests accept Idempotency-Key header for safe retries
  >> 6.2 Authentication API
  >> Method
  >> Endpoint
  >> Body
  >> Response
  >> POST
  >> /auth/otp/send
  >> { phone: string }
  >> { otp_id: string, expires_in: 300 }
  >> Public
  >> /auth/otp/verify
  >> { otp_id, otp: string }
  >> { access_token, refresh_token, user }
  >> /auth/token/refresh
  >> { refresh_token }
  >> { access_token, refresh_token }
  >> /auth/logout
  >> { success: true }
  >> Bearer
  >> /auth/me
  >> { user: UserProfile }
  >> 6.3 Farm Management API
  >> /farms
  >> Create a new farm
  >> List all farms for authenticated farmer
  >> /farms/:id
  >> Farmer/Admin
  >> Get farm details
  >> PATCH
  >> Farmer (owner)
  >> Update farm details
  >> DELETE
  >> Soft-delete farm
  >> /farms/:id/ponds
  >> Add pond to farm
  >> List ponds for farm
  >> /ponds/:id
  >> Update pond details
  >> /ponds/:id/crops
  >> Start new crop cycle
  >> List crop cycles
  >> /ponds/:id/crops/active
  >> Get current active crop
  >> /crops/:id/harvest
  >> Mark crop as harvested
  >> /crops/:id/feed-logs
  >> Log feed entry
  >> List feed logs
  >> /crops/:id/mortality-logs
  >> Log mortality event
  >> /crops/:id/water-logs
  >> Log water quality
  >> /farmer/dashboard
  >> Aggregated farm dashboard data
  >> 6.4 Harvest Marketplace API
  >> /harvest-listings
  >> Create harvest listing
  >> Public (limited)
  >> Search harvest listings
  >> /harvest-listings/:id

  >> 7. UI/UX Design System
  >> 7.1 Design Philosophy
  >> Principle
  >> Implementation
  >> Telugu First
  >> All UI strings in Telugu by default; English toggle in settings
  >> Large Touch Targets
  >> Minimum 48×48dp tap targets; primary actions ≥ 56dp height
  >> High Contrast
  >> WCAG AA compliant contrast ratios for outdoor readability
  >> Offline-First
  >> All critical screens load from local SQLite cache when offline
  >> Progressive Disclosure
  >> Show only essential info; detail on tap — no cognitive overload
  >> Skeleton Loading
  >> All data loads show skeleton UI — never blank white screens
  >> Error Recovery
  >> Every error state has a clear retry action and human-readable message in Telugu
  >> Minimal Input
  >> Smart defaults, autocomplete, toggles over free text wherever possible
  >> Data Light
  >> All API responses optimised for < 10KB; images lazy loaded
  >> 7.2 Design Tokens

  >> 8. Security Architecture
  >> Security Standard: OWASP Top 10 compliance + India DPDP Act 2023 compliance
  >> 8.1 Authentication & Authorization
  >> Authentication Method
  >> OTP-based (phone number) — no passwords to steal or forget
  >> OTP Provider
  >> MSG91 with 6-digit OTP, 5-minute expiry
  >> OTP Rate Limiting
  >> Max 3 OTPs per phone per 15 minutes; 10 per day
  >> Token Type
  >> JWT (RS256 signed) — asymmetric signing, public key verification
  >> Access Token TTL
  >> 15 minutes — short-lived to limit exposure window
  >> Refresh Token TTL
  >> 30 days — rotated on each use (refresh token rotation)
  >> Refresh Token Storage
  >> Stored in device secure storage (Flutter Secure Storage)
  >> Token Blacklist
  >> Upstash Redis stores invalidated JTIs for immediate logout
  >> Role System
  >> RBAC: farmer, buyer, supplier, advisor, admin — enforced at API Gateway
  >> Row-Level Security
  >> Database queries include user_id filter; no trust in client-side IDs
  >> 8.2 API Security
  >> Transport
  >> TLS 1.3 minimum; HSTS enforced; HTTP → HTTPS redirect
  >> Per-user: 100 req/min; Per-IP: 500 req/min; Login: 5 attempts/15min
  >> API Gateway WAF
  >> AWS WAF with OWASP Core Rule Set — blocks SQLi, XSS, RCE patterns
  >> CORS
  >> Strict allowlist: app://aquaos, https://admin.aquaos.in only
  >> Input Validation
  >> All inputs validated with Zod schemas before processing
  >> SQL Injection
  >> Parameterised queries only (Drizzle ORM); no raw SQL with user input
  >> Request Signing
  >> Mobile app signs critical requests with device keypair (Phase 2)
  >> Fraud Detection
  >> Unusual patterns (bulk offer submissions, fake listings) flagged and reviewed
  >> Content Security
  >> File uploads: MIME type validation + virus scan (ClamAV Lambda layer)
  >> 8.3 Data Privacy (DPDP Act 2023 Compliance)
  >> Data Minimisation
  >> Collect only fields required for stated purpose
  >> Consent Recording
  >> Explicit consent captured at registration; stored with timestamp
  >> Location Privacy
  >> Farm GPS stored encrypted; not shared without farmer consent
  >> Data Subject Rights
  >> In-app: Download My Data + Delete My Account (30-day deletion)
  >> Third-Party Sharing
  >> Only with buyer/supplier as part of transaction; disclosed in ToS
  >> Data Retention
  >> Active: indefinite; Deleted accounts: 30-day soft delete then purge
  >> Data Protection Officer role defined; contact in app settings
  >> Breach Response
  >> 72-hour notification to CERT-In and affected users per DPDP Act
  >> 8.4 Infrastructure Security
  >> Secrets Management
  >> AWS Secrets Manager — no secrets in environment variables or code
  >> VPC Isolation
  >> Lambda functions in private VPC; database not publicly accessible
  >> Database Access
  >> Only Lambda VPC security group allowed; no direct internet access
  >> Encryption at Rest
  >> PlanetScale: encrypted at rest (AES-256); R2: SSE enabled
  >> Encryption in Transit
  >> TLS 1.3 for all service-to-service communication
  >> IAM Least Privilege
  >> Each Lambda has minimal IAM permissions; no admin roles
  >> Dependency Scanning
  >> GitHub Dependabot scans all dependencies; critical CVEs → immediate patch
  >> Security Headers
  >> CSP, X-Frame-Options, X-Content-Type-Options on all responses
  >> Audit Logging
  >> All admin actions logged to append-only Axiom log stream
  >> 8.5 Farmer Data Privacy Controls
  >> Farm Location
  >> Toggle: Show district only | Show village | Show GPS (default: district only)
  >> Production Volume
  >> Toggle: Hide total harvest volume from public (default: hidden)
  >> Contact Details
  >> Toggle: Allow buyers to see phone after offer accepted (default: after acceptance)
  >> Community Identity
  >> Toggle: Show farm name in community | Anonymous posts
  >> Data Analytics
  >> Toggle: Contribute anonymous farm data to industry analytics

  >> < 2 seconds

  >> < 20MB APK download
  >> Flutter build size analysis
  >> API Availability
  >> 99.9% uptime
  >> UptimeRobot monitoring
  >> Lambda Cold Start

  >> AWS X-Ray
  >> 9.2 Caching Strategy
  >> Data Type
  >> Invalidation Strategy
  >> Farm Dashboard
  >> Upstash Redis (server-side)
  >> 5 minutes
  >> Write-through invalidation on any farm/crop write
  >> Daily Prices
  >> 1 hour
  >> Price update job clears cache
  >> Product Listings
  >> Meilisearch index
  >> Real-time sync via DB trigger
  >> Add/update product → re-index
  >> Harvest Listings
  >> Real-time sync
  >> Listing create/update → re-index
  >> User Profiles
  >> 30 minutes
  >> Profile update → clear user cache
  >> Advisory Rules
  >> Lambda memory (in-process)
  >> Lambda lifetime (~15min)
  >> Advisory service redeploy on rule change
  >> Static Assets
  >> Cloudflare CDN
  >> 1 year (versioned URLs)
  >> URL-based cache busting on deploy
  >> App Bundle
  >> Device local storage
  >> Until app update
  >> Flutter incremental update
  >> 9.3 Scalability Design
  >> Compute Scaling
  >> AWS Lambda: concurrent executions scale from 0 to 10,000 automatically
  >> Database Scaling
  >> PlanetScale: auto-scales read replicas; sharding ready for 1B+ rows
  >> Search Scaling
  >> Meilisearch: horizontal scaling via multiple instances on Fly.io
  >> CDN Scaling
  >> Cloudflare: global edge network handles any traffic volume
  >> Chat Scaling
  >> Supabase Realtime: 200 concurrent on free; upgrade to Pro at 10K MAU for $25/month
  >> Storage Scaling
  >> Cloudflare R2: unlimited storage, no egress cost — scales infinitely
  >> Notification Scaling
  >> FCM: Google's infrastructure handles millions/second natively
  >> Database Connection Pooling
  >> PlanetScale serverless driver — no connection pool exhaustion
  >> 9.4 Offline Architecture
  >> Feature
  >> Offline Capability
  >> Sync Strategy
  >> Full offline from local SQLite cache
  >> Background sync on connectivity restore
  >> Feed Logging
  >> Full offline — stores locally
  >> Queued sync with conflict resolution (last-write-wins)
  >> Mortality Logging
  >> Queued sync on connectivity restore
  >> Water Quality Logging
  >> Advisory Alerts
  >> Shows last-received alerts from cache
  >> New alerts delivered when online
  >> Market Prices
  >> Last 24h prices cached locally
  >> Refresh on connectivity
  >> View only from cache; create requires connectivity
  >> Sync when online
  >> Community Posts
  >> View cached posts; post creation requires connectivity
  >> Draft saved locally
  >> Chat
  >> Offline reads; sends queued
  >> Queue processed on connectivity
  >> 10. DevOps, Infrastructure & Deployment
  >> 10.1 Infrastructure-as-Code
  >> IaC Tool
  >> AWS CDK v2 (TypeScript)

  >> dev, staging, production — identical stacks, different configs

  >> AWS Secrets Manager (API keys, DB credentials, JWT signing keys)
  >> Deployment Command
  >> cdk deploy --all (deploys all stacks in dependency order)
  >> Stack Separation
  >> VPC Stack → Auth Stack → Database Stack → API Stack → Frontend Stack

  >> Steps

  >> PR Check

  >> < 8 min

  >> Tag release (v*.*.*)
  >> Build + E2E tests + CDK deploy + Slack notification
  >> < 12 min

  >> Tag release or manual trigger

  >> < 15 min
  >> Rollback
  >> Manual trigger or automatic on smoke test fail
  >> CDK deploy previous version
  >> < 5 min

  >> Application Logs

  >> Performance Monitoring
  >> AWS X-Ray — traces request flow across Lambda + database
  >> Business Metrics
  >> Mixpanel — farmer DAU, listing creation rate, offer acceptance rate
  >> Database Monitoring
  >> PlanetScale built-in query insights; slow query alerts
  >> Cost Monitoring
  >> AWS Cost Explorer + budget alerts at $10, $50, $100 thresholds
  >> Alerting Channel
  >> Slack #ops-alerts for warnings; PagerDuty for critical (downtime)

  >> 13. Admin Panel Specification
  >> 13.1 Admin Dashboard Overview
  >> 13.2 Admin Module Breakdown
  >> User Management
  >> View
  >> All users with filters: role, district, registration date, verification status
  >> Actions
  >> Verify farmer, verify supplier, suspend user, impersonate (read-only) for support
  >> KYC Queue
  >> Unverified suppliers sorted by registration date; approve/reject with note
  >> Fraud Flags
  >> Users flagged by system (fake listings, bulk operations) for review
  >> Harvest Listings Monitoring
  >> All active listings with status, district, species, price deviation from market
  >> Remove listing (with reason notification to farmer), flag for review
  >> Price Integrity
  >> Listings with price > 30% above/below market auto-flagged for review
  >> Supplier Verification
  >> Queue
  >> New supplier registrations with GSTIN, license upload, business proof
  >> Admin verifies GSTIN via GST portal API + license authenticity
  >> Outcome
  >> Approve (live in marketplace) / Reject (with reason) / Request more info
  >> Community Moderation
  >> Report Queue
  >> Posts/comments reported by community, sorted by report count
  >> Remove post, warn user, suspend user (7 days / 30 days / permanent)
  >> Auto-Flagged
  >> Posts with 3+ reports auto-hidden pending review
  >> Keyword Filter
  >> Configurable blocked keyword list (scam, competitor brand attacks, etc.)
  >> Platform Analytics Dashboard
  >> Farmer Metrics
  >> Daily registrations, MAU, crop cycles started, feed logs, dashboard opens
  >> Marketplace Metrics
  >> Listings created, offers submitted, acceptance rate, GMV by day/district
  >> Supplier Metrics
  >> Inquiries sent, conversion rate, top products by views
  >> Advisory Metrics
  >> Alerts generated, acknowledgement rate, alert types distribution
  >> Revenue Metrics
  >> Active subscriptions, commission collected, MRR growth
  >> Geographic Heatmap
  >> Farmer density + activity by district on AP map
  >> Advisory Rule Management
  >> Rule Editor
  >> No-code rule builder: IF [metric] [operator] [value] THEN [alert type] [message]
  >> A/B Testing
  >> Test two alert messages; track acknowledgement rate
  >> Rule History
  >> Audit log of all rule changes with author + timestamp

  >> 14.2 Event Tracking Plan
  >> Event Name
  >> Properties
  >> farm_created
  >> Farmer creates first farm
  >> district, total_area, water_source
  >> pond_added
  >> Pond added to farm
  >> area, farm_id, pond_count (total)
  >> crop_started
  >> Crop cycle started
  >> species, seed_count, pond_area, stocking_density
  >> feed_logged
  >> Feed entry submitted
  >> brand, quantity_kg, crop_age, was_reminder_triggered
  >> mortality_logged
  >> Mortality log submitted
  >> count, symptoms[], mortality_pct_of_stock
  >> advisory_alert_shown
  >> Alert displayed to farmer
  >> alert_type, severity, crop_age
  >> advisory_alert_acknowledged
  >> Farmer taps 'Got It'
  >> alert_id, time_to_ack_minutes
  >> harvest_listing_created
  >> Listing published
  >> species, size_count, quantity_kg, has_price, has_photos
  >> offer_submitted
  >> Buyer submits offer
  >> listing_id, offered_price, quantity
  >> offer_accepted
  >> Farmer accepts offer
  >> listing_id, final_price, negotiation_rounds
  >> product_inquiry_sent
  >> Farmer sends supplier inquiry
  >> product_id, category, quantity
  >> community_post_created
  >> Post published
  >> type, has_images, tag, language
  >> market_price_viewed
  >> Price screen opened
  >> species, district
  >> search_performed
  >> Buyer/farmer performs search
  >> query_type, filters_applied, results_count
  >> 14.3 Regional Intelligence Reports
  >> District Supply Forecast
  >> Upcoming harvest volumes by species, size, district — 14-day forward view
  >> Disease Outbreak Heatmap
  >> Anonymous mortality spike clustering by district and symptom
  >> Input Price Index
  >> Average input prices by category across all listed suppliers
  >> Feed Efficiency Benchmark
  >> Average FCR by species, district, season — anonymised
  >> Survival Rate Trends
  >> Survival rates over time — useful for MPEDA and insurance providers
  >> Harvest Price Index
  >> Weighted average transaction prices by species/size/district

  >> 16.4 Technical Debt Prevention Rules
  >> The following rules are enforced from Day 1 of development to prevent compounding technical debt:
  >> TypeScript Strict Mode
  >> tsconfig strict: true — no implicit any, strict null checks
  >> Test Coverage
  >> Minimum 70% coverage on all service layers; 90% on payment flows
  >> API Documentation
  >> OpenAPI 3.0 spec auto-generated and kept in sync; no API without docs
  >> Database Migrations
  >> All schema changes via PlanetScale branches — no direct schema edits
  >> Code Review
  >> No PR merged without 1 approval; Tech Lead reviews all schema changes
  >> Dependency Policy
  >> All new dependencies require Tech Lead sign-off; no abandoned packages
  >> Performance Budget
  >> API responses must include execution time header; fail CI if > 2000ms
  >> Error Handling
  >> All async functions wrapped in try/catch; no silent failures
  >> Logging Standards
  >> Structured JSON logs with correlation IDs; no console.log in production
  >> Feature Flags
  >> All new features behind flags (Growthbook free tier); safe rollout
  >> 17. Legal, Compliance & Risk Management
  >> 17.1 Regulatory Compliance
  >> India DPDP Act 2023
  >> Full compliance: consent capture, data minimisation, erasure rights, DPO appointed
  >> IT Act 2000
  >> Platform intermediary protections; grievance officer contact in app
  >> FSSAI
  >> Food safety compliance for any platform-facilitated food transactions
  >> Marine Products (MPEDA)
  >> Harvest listings do not facilitate uncertified exports; advisory only
  >> GST Compliance
  >> Platform commission invoices with GST; marketplace participants responsible for own GST
  >> RBI Payment Regulations
  >> Razorpay handles PCI-DSS compliance; platform does not store card data
  >> Consumer Protection Act 2019
  >> Dispute resolution mechanism built into platform; 30-day resolution SLA
  >> 17.2 Risk Register
  >> Risk
  >> Probability
  >> Impact
  >> Mitigation
  >> Farmer churn — low engagement
  >> Medium
  >> High
  >> Daily reminders, offline-first, Telugu UI, Champions program
  >> Fake harvest listings
  >> Verified farmer badges, crop cycle linkage, admin monitoring
  >> Supplier fraud (counterfeit products)
  >> GSTIN verification, license check, community reviews, report system
  >> Data breach
  >> Very High
  >> Encryption, WAF, minimal data collection, incident response plan
  >> OTP fraud / SIM swap
  >> Device binding (Phase 2), suspicious login alerts
  >> Payment dispute (harvest)
  >> Escrow option (Phase 2), in-app chat evidence, dispute resolution
  >> Regulatory change (aquaculture policy)
  >> Stay updated with MPEDA/state dept; modular advisory content
  >> AWS cost spike (traffic spike)
  >> Budget alerts, Lambda concurrency limits, cost monitoring
  >> App store rejection
  >> Follow Google Play policies strictly; review guidelines before release
  >> Competitor cloning
  >> Network effects moat, data moat, farmer trust is hardest to clone
  >> 17.3 Terms of Service Key Points
  >> Platform Role
  >> Intermediary — not a party to buyer-seller transactions
  >> Farmer Data Ownership
  >> Farmer owns their farm data; can export or delete at any time
  >> Dispute Liability
  >> Platform not liable for transaction disputes; facilitates resolution
  >> Content Moderation
  >> Platform may remove content violating community guidelines
  >> Price Transparency
  >> Platform does not fix prices; all prices are farmer/buyer negotiated
  >> Commission Disclosure
  >> Commission rates clearly disclosed before transaction completion

  >> Integration with YSI, Hanna Instruments, local APEDA-certified sensor manufacturers
  >> Cost Model
  >> Sensor hardware subsidised by platform (₹2,000–5,000/pond); subscription offsets
  >> 18.3 Financial Services Integration
  >> Crop Loan Facilitation
  >> Farm data as creditworthiness signal → NBFC partnerships for pre-approved crop loans
  >> Crop Insurance
  >> Automatic insurance quote based on crop data + weather risk → single-tap insurance purchase
  >> Input Credit
  >> Buy-now-pay-at-harvest model for feed purchases → solved with NBFC partner
  >> Harvest Advance
  >> Confirmed harvest listing → advance payment from buyer (5–7 days before harvest)
  >> Savings Product
  >> Partner bank savings account with aquaculture-season-aware sweep features

  >> 19.1 Glossary
  >> Term
  >> Post-Larvae — juvenile shrimp ready for stocking, counted per thousand
  >> Dissolved Oxygen — critical water quality parameter; optimal 5–8 mg/L for shrimp
  >> Vannamei
  >> Litopenaeus vannamei — Pacific Whiteleg Shrimp; 80%+ of AP production
  >> Shrimp size expressed as number per kilogram (e.g. 30-count = 30 shrimp per kg)
  >> Gross Merchandise Value — total value of transactions through platform
  >> Monthly Active Users
  >> MPEDA
  >> Marine Products Export Development Authority — central govt seafood regulator
  >> DPDP Act
  >> Digital Personal Data Protection Act 2023 — India's primary data privacy law
  >> AWS Cloud Development Kit — IaC tool for defining AWS infrastructure in TypeScript
  >> JSON Web Token — stateless authentication token
  >> RBAC
  >> Role-Based Access Control — permission system based on user roles
  >> Monthly Recurring Revenue — subscription revenue earned each month
  >> Net Promoter Score — measure of user satisfaction and likelihood to recommend
  >> Web Application Firewall — security layer filtering malicious HTTP traffic
  >> Time-to-Live — duration for which cached data is considered valid

AQUAOS
Aquaculture Ecosystem Platform
Product Requirements Document
Farm OS  ·  Advisory Engine  ·  Input Marketplace  ·  Harvest Marketplace  ·  Farmer Community
Primary Launch Geography: Andhra Pradesh, India
Version

Classification
Confidential
Launch Target
Q3 2025 — Andhra Pradesh
Architecture  ·  Security  ·  UI/UX  ·  API  ·  Database  ·  DevOps  ·  Monetization
1. Executive Summary
AquaOS is a mobile-first, serverless aquaculture operating system purpose-built for India's rapidly expanding shrimp and fish farming industry, with an initial focus on the high-density aquaculture districts of Andhra Pradesh. The platform eliminates the four chronic pain-points of Indian aquaculture: information asymmetry, input procurement inefficiency, harvest price opacity, and operational data blindness.
Mission: Empower every aquaculture farmer in India with enterprise-grade tools, fair market access, and intelligent advisory — free of cost, forever.
1.1 The Opportunity
India is the second-largest shrimp producer globally, with Andhra Pradesh contributing over 70% of national aquaculture output. Yet 80% of farmers operate without any digital tools, rely on middlemen for both inputs and harvest sales, and receive no real-time market pricing data. The average farmer loses 22–35% of potential income to inefficiency. AquaOS captures this value and distributes it back to farmers, while monetising the ecosystem through buyer subscriptions, supplier listings, and transaction commissions.
1.2 Core Value Propositions
Stakeholder
Core Value Delivered
Measurable Impact
Farmer
Free digital farm OS + market access + advisory
+18–30% net income

Direct verified harvest listings + real-time offers
−15% procurement cost

+35% conversion rate

₹200Cr+ GMV Year 3

Supply chain efficiency
1.3 Zero-Cost Infrastructure Model
The platform is architected on a 100% serverless, pay-per-use model. During pre-revenue phases, cloud costs approximate ₹0 for workloads under free-tier thresholds. As revenue scales, infrastructure scales proportionally with near-zero fixed overhead. This eliminates the burn-rate trap that kills agri-tech startups.

AWS (primary) with multi-cloud readiness

AWS Lambda — 1M requests/month free forever

  >> India's property market is deeply broken across five dimensions:
  >> 1. Urban Renters pay 1–2 months' brokerage (₹10,000–₹60,000) for every house move —
  >> 2. Agricultural Landowners have NO digital platform to list, lease, or sell farm land — relying
  >> 3. Rural Migrants moving to cities for work have zero trusted platform to find affordable PG
  >> 4. Property Owners (NRI & Local) struggle to find verified tenants and manage rent
  >> 5. Society Admins have fragmented tools for visitor management, complaint tracking,
  >> 1.3 The FarmerConnect Solution
  >> A unified, AI-first, zero-broker property marketplace that serves:
  >> Urban rental seekers
  >> Agricultural land seekers and owners
  >> PG/co-living seekers
  >> Society communities
  >> Property managers and NRI landlords

  >> Uniquely covers agricultural + urban properties (no competitor does both)

  >> Built on ₹0/month infrastructure (Supabase + Cloudflare + Vercel)
  >> Bank-grade security without enterprise cost
  >> Vernacular-first (Telugu, Kannada, Hindi, Tamil alongside English)

  >> 3.2 Mission
  >> Build a platform so trustworthy and simple that a farmer in rural Andhra Pradesh can list his 5-
  >> acre land for lease with the same confidence as a Bengaluru techie finding a 2BHK — in their
  >> 3.3 Core Design Principles
  >> Principle 	Meaning in Practice
  >> Trust First 	Every user, listing, and transaction is verified before going live
  >> Zero Friction 	Any key action (search, contact, pay) completes in ≤3 taps
  >> Privacy by Default 	Phone numbers never exposed; calls go through masked numbers
  >> Vernacular Native 	No user should be disadvantaged by their language
  >> Offline Resilient 	Core search and viewing works without internet
  >> Transparent Pricing 	No hidden fees; all charges shown upfront before confirmation
  >> Data Sovereignty 	User data never sold; DPDP Act 2023 compliant by design
  >> SECTION 4 — BUSINESS MODEL & REVENUE ARCHITECTURE
  >> 4.1 Revenue Streams
  >> Stream 1: Subscription Plans (Primary)
  >> For Property Seekers (Tenants/Buyers):
  >> Plan 	Price 	Duration Features
  >> Free 	₹0 	Always 	Browse, shortlist, 3 contacts/month
  >> Connect ₹499 	30 days 	Unlimited contacts, chat, visit scheduling
  >> Relax 	₹1,499 90 days 	RM-assisted search, priority matching, home visits arranged
  >> Power 	₹2,999 180 days All of Relax + legal agreement included, background check of owner
  >> For Property Owners/Landlords:
  >> Free 	₹0 	Always 	1 active listing, basic photos
  >> Premium ₹799 	90 days 	5 listings, featured placement, unlimited leads
  >> Pro 	₹1,999 180 days 	15 listings, top of search, RM support, verified badge
  >> Elite 	₹4,999 365 days 	Unlimited listings, dedicated RM, monthly reports, NRI support
  >> For Agricultural Land Owners:
  >> Plan 	Price 	Duration 	Features
  >> Basic 	₹0 	Always 	1 land listing, basic details
  >> AgriPro 	₹1,499 	180 days 	5 listings, verified badge, priority in agri search
  >> AgriElite 	₹3,999 	365 days 	Unlimited listings, legal support, yield data integration
  >> Stream 2: Transaction Fees (Secondary)
  >> Service 	Fee 	Trigger
  >> Digital Rent Agreement 	₹399–₹2,499 	User initiates agreement
  >> Digital Land Lease Agreement 	₹599–₹3,499 	User initiates agri agreement
  >> E-stamp (pass-through) 	State stamp duty 	Agreement execution
  >> Rent Payment Processing 	1.5% of rent (capped ₹999) 	Successful rent payment
  >> Background Verification 	₹199–₹599 	KYC verification request
  >> Packers & Movers Referral 	5–8% commission 	Completed booking
  >> Stream 3: Advertising & Promotions (Tertiary)
  >> Product 	Description 	Price Range
  >> Featured Listing 	Top placement in search results 	₹299–₹999/listing/week
  >> Homepage Banner 	Property developer banners 	₹10,000–₹50,000/week
  >> Locality Spotlight 	Builder pins on map 	₹5,000–₹20,000/month
  >> Push Notification Ads 	Targeted push to seekers 	₹2/notification
  >> Stream 4: B2B SaaS (Society Management)
  >> Module 	Fee 	Billing
  >> Society Management Suite 	₹50–₹150/unit/month 	Monthly
  >> Visitor Management 	₹30/unit/month 	Monthly
  >> Maintenance Collection 	1% of collection 	Per transaction
  >> Community Commerce 	8% commission 	Per order
  >> 4.2 Revenue Projection (Conservative)
  >> Year 	Users 	Paying Users (5%) 	ARPU (₹/year) 	Total Revenue
  >> Yr 1 	1,00,000 	5,000 	₹1,800 	₹90 Lakhs
  >> Yr 2 	10,00,000 	75,000 	₹2,400 	₹18 Crores
  >> Yr 3 	50,00,000 	5,00,000 	₹3,200 	₹160 Crores
  >> Yr 5 	2,00,00,000 	30,00,000 	₹4,000 	₹1,200 Crores
  >> 4.3 Unit Economics
  >> CAC (Customer Acquisition Cost): ₹45–₹80 (organic SEO + referral-first)
  >> LTV (Lifetime Value): ₹3,200–₹8,400 (3–7 year average tenure)
  >> LTV:CAC Ratio Target: 40:1
  >> Gross Margin: 82–88% (software-only, minimal ops)

  >> SECTION 6 — CORE FEATURE MODULES — DETAILED
  >> SPECIFICATIONS
  >> Module 1: User Onboarding & KYC
  >> 1.1 Registration Flow
  >> Step 1: Enter phone number → OTP (Supabase Auth / MSG91)
  >> Step 2: Select role (Tenant / Owner / Farmer / PG Seeker / Society Admin / Broker)
  >> 1.2 KYC Data Collected by Role
  >> Role 	Required Documents
  >> Tenant 	Aadhaar (masked), Selfie liveness check
  >> Owner 	Aadhaar + PAN + Property document (sale deed / khata / EC)
  >> Farmer 	Aadhaar + Patta/ROR (Record of Rights) + Land passbook
  >> Broker 	Aadhaar + PAN + RERA registration number
  >> Society Admin 	Aadhaar + Society registration document + Election proof
  >> 1.3 KYC Verification Process
  >> 1.4 Notification on KYC
  >> SMS + WhatsApp + In-app push on status change
  >> Rejection includes specific reason and document re-upload link
  >> Verified owners receive automated listing approval fast-track
  >> Step 3: Basic profile (Name, profile photo, city)
  >> Step 4: Role-specific questions
  >> Step 5: KYC initiation (optional at registration, mandatory for posting/paying)
  >> 1. User uploads documents via in-app camera (no third-party redirect)
  >> 2. System runs OCR extraction (Tesseract / AWS Textract free tier)
  >> 3. Automated face match: selfie vs Aadhaar photo (DigiLocker integration)
  >> 4. Automated RERA validation (RERA API for brokers)
  >> 5. AI risk score assigned (0–100): documents quality, match confidence, fraud
  >> signals
  >> 6. Score > 80: Auto-approved
  >> 7. Score 50–80: Manual review by verification agent (SLA: 4 hours)
  >> 8. Score < 50: Rejected with reason + re-upload option
  >> 9. KYC status: Pending → In Review → Verified / Rejected
  >> 10. Verified badge shown on profile and listings
  >> Module 2: Property Search & Discovery
  >> 2.1 Search Architecture
  >> 2.2 Filter Taxonomy
  >> For Residential Rental:
  >> Property type: Flat, Independent House, Villa, Row House
  >> BHK: 1RK, 1BHK, 2BHK, 3BHK, 4BHK, 4BHK+
  >> Rent range: Slider (₹3,000 – ₹5,00,000)
  >> Furnishing: Unfurnished, Semi-Furnished, Fully Furnished
  >> Floor: Ground, Low (1–4), Mid (5–10), High (10+), Penthouse
  >> Facing: East, North, West, South
  >> Available from: Date picker
  >> Pet friendly: Yes/No/Negotiable
  >> Parking: 2W / 4W / Both / None
  >> Lift: Yes/No
  >> Society: Gated / Non-Gated
  >> Verified only: Toggle
  >> Owner-direct only: Toggle
  >> Input Layer:
  >> - Text search (property name, locality, landmark)
  >> - Voice search (vernacular: Telugu, Hindi, Kannada, Tamil)
  >> - Map-based drag-to-search
  >> - AI-assisted: "2BHK near Miyapur metro under ₹15,000"
  >> Processing Layer (Supabase + pgvector):
  >> - Full-text search index on listings (tsvector)
  >> - Vector embeddings for semantic similarity search
  >> - Geospatial PostGIS queries for radius/polygon search
  >> - Real-time inventory check (Supabase Realtime)
  >> Results Layer:
  >> - Relevance ranking: AI score × recency × completeness × verification
  >> - Personalized ranking: user preference model
  >> - Sponsored insertion: 1 in 10 positions
  >> For Agricultural Land:
  >> Land type: Agricultural, Orchard, Plantation, Fallow, Converted
  >> Purpose: Lease, Sale, Joint Farming, Mortgage
  >> Area: Slider (0.5 acres – 500 acres)
  >> Soil type: Red, Black (Cotton), Alluvial, Sandy, Laterite
  >> Water source: Borewell, Canal, Drip, Rain-fed, River
  >> District / Mandal / Village (cascading dropdown)
  >> Survey number (text search)
  >> Price: Per acre per year (lease) or per acre (sale)
  >> Crop suitability: Paddy, Cotton, Chilli, Mango, Sugarcane, Groundnut, Tomato
  >> For PG/Co-living:
  >> Gender preference: Boys / Girls / Mixed
  >> Room type: Single / Double / Triple / Dormitory
  >> Meal plan: With meals / Without meals / Optional
  >> Amenities: WiFi, AC, Laundry, TV, Gym, Swimming pool
  >> College/company nearby (tag-based)
  >> Monthly fee range
  >> Deposit amount
  >> Notice period: 30 days / 15 days / None
