  >> Step 2: Photos & Media Upload
  >> Step 3: Property Details
  >> Step 4: Pricing
  >> Step 5: Preferences
  >> - Property type (Flat / House / Villa / Land / PG / Commercial)
  >> - Transaction type (Rent / Sale / Lease)
  >> - BHK selection
  >> - City → Locality (autocomplete with MapBox)
  >> - Society/Building name (optional autocomplete)
  >> - Floor & Total floors
  >> - Built-up area & Carpet area
  >> - Minimum 5 photos required
  >> - Maximum 50 photos
  >> - Auto-enhancement: brightness, sharpness correction via Cloudflare Images
  >> - Mandatory: Living room, bedroom, bathroom, kitchen, exterior
  >> - Optional: Floor plan upload (PDF/Image)
  >> - 360° virtual tour embed (Matterport link, optional)
  >> - Video tour (up to 3 min, compressed via Cloudflare Stream)
  >> - AI auto-caption generation for each photo
  >> - Furnishing status (unfurnished / semi / fully)
  >> - Amenities checklist (50+ options with icons)
  >> - Facing direction
  >> - Age of property (slider)
  >> - Maintenance fee (per month)
  >> - Available from (date)
  >> - Parking details
  >> - Society features (gym, pool, clubhouse, security, power backup)
  >> - Monthly rent (with market benchmark shown)
  >> - Security deposit (with legal max shown: 2–3 months)
  >> - Brokerage: ZERO (platform-enforced for owner listings)
  >> - Any other charges (Society maintenance, water)
  >> - AI suggested price: "Based on 47 similar properties, ₹22,000–₹26,000"
  >> Step 6: Preview & Publish
  >> 3.2 Listing Verification Process
  >> 3.3 Listing States & Lifecycle
  >> - Who can contact: Anyone / Verified Only / Families Only / Bachelors / Working
  >> Professionals
  >> - Pet policy
  >> - Smoking policy
  >> - Religion preference: HIDDEN from seekers (for compliance); used only for
  >> algorithmic soft-preference
  >> - Preferred tenant occupation
  >> - Full listing preview in seeker view
  >> - Completeness score shown: "87% complete – Add 2 more photos for Premium badge"
  >> - Estimated visibility score
  >> - Publish → goes to Verification queue
  >> - Expected approval time shown (auto-approve if owner is KYC-verified Level 2+)
  >> Auto-checks (instant):
  >> ✅ Photo clarity (AI model: blur detection, inappropriate content)
  >> ✅ Rent reasonableness (vs. locality benchmark ± 3 SD)
  >> ✅ Description spam check (no phone numbers, no "WhatsApp", no broker language)
  >> ✅ Duplicate listing detection (cosine similarity on address + rent + photos)
  >> ✅ Owner KYC status
  >> Manual checks (verification agent, SLA 2 hours):
  >> ✅ Property ownership document cross-check
  >> ✅ Society name / building verification (Google Maps API)
  >> ✅ Photo relevance (is this actually the property?)
  >> ✅ Pricing abuse check (far below market = potential scam)
  >> Post-verification:
  >> → Approved: Goes live + owner notified
  >> → Rejected: Reason given + edit option
  >> → Suspended: For repeated violations (account-level flag)
  >> Draft → Under Review → Active → Shortlisted (by seekers) →
  >> Contact Unlocked → Visit Scheduled → Negotiating →
  >> Deal Confirmed / Relisted / Expired
  >> 3.4 Listing Expiry & Refresh
  >> Standard listings expire after 90 days
  >> System sends Day-75, Day-85, Day-89 reminders
  >> One-tap refresh (re-verification if price/details unchanged)
  >> Auto-expire prevents stale inventory pollution
  >> Module 4: Communication (Chat, Calls, Number Masking)
  >> 4.1 Chat System
  >> 4.2 Number Masking & Call System
  >> Architecture: Supabase Realtime (WebSocket)
  >> Storage: Supabase PostgreSQL (messages table)
  >> File sharing: Cloudflare R2 (photos, documents)
  >> Encryption: End-to-end encrypted via Signal Protocol (libsodium)
  >> Features:
  >> - One-to-one chat between seeker and owner
  >> - Typing indicators, read receipts
  >> - Message reactions (shorthand responses)
  >> - Photo/document sharing
  >> - Quick replies: "Is property still available?" / "Can I visit tomorrow?" / "What
  >> is maintenance?"
  >> - Auto-translate (vernacular ↔ English via LibreTranslate)
  >> - AI-assisted response suggestions for owners
  >> - Spam detection: block if > 5 unsolicited contacts/day
  >> - Report & Block functionality
  >> - Chat archival after deal confirmed or 90 days
  >> Architecture: Exotel (free starter) / Twilio / MSG91 (pay-as-you-go)
  >> Zero fixed cost: pay only per call minute (~₹0.25/min)
  >> Flow:
  >> 1. Seeker clicks "Call Owner"
  >> 2. System allocates temp virtual number (masked)
  >> 3. Seeker's phone dials virtual number
  >> 4. System bridges call to owner's real number
  >> 5. Neither party sees the other's real number
  >> 4.3 Communication Rules (Platform Policy)
  >> Phone numbers NEVER shared in chat or listing description (auto-redacted by AI)
  >> Minimum 1 KYC tier (phone-verified) required to initiate contact
  >> Contact unlock costs one "credit" (included in paid plans or ₹9/credit free tier)
  >> Anti-spam: ML model detects broker solicitation language → auto-flag
  >> Module 5: Payments & Financial Infrastructure
  >> 5.1 Payment Architecture (Zero-INR Stack)
  >> 5.2 Rent Payment Flow
  >> 6. Call recorded (stored 90 days, accessible for disputes)
  >> 7. Call log stored: duration, time, listing, outcome
  >> Alternatives (Zero Cost):
  >> - In-app VoIP (WebRTC via Agora free tier: 10,000 min/month free)
  >> - WhatsApp Business API trigger (for ₹0 on template messages)
  >> Primary Gateway: Razorpay (pay-per-transaction, 2% + GST)
  >> Backup Gateway: Cashfree Payments (pay-per-transaction)
  >> UPI: Native UPI via both gateways
  >> Cards: Visa, Mastercard, Rupay
  >> Netbanking: All major banks
  >> Wallets: Paytm, PhonePe (via gateway)
  >> EMI: Bajaj, HDFC, ICICI (for large deposits)
  >> BNPL: LazyPay, ZestMoney
  >> Cost Model:
  >> - Platform absorbs 0% of transaction fees for subscription payments
  >> - Transaction fee passed to user (transparently shown): 2% for cards/NB, 0% for
  >> - UPI preferred (zero cost) — default payment method
  >> 1. Tenant adds property (owner bank details or UPI)
  >> 2. System validates owner bank via penny-drop (₹1 test transfer)
  >> 3. Tenant selects amount, chooses payment method
  >> 4. Payment captured by Razorpay
  >> 5. After T+2 (settlement cycle): transferred to owner bank
  >> 5.3 Subscription Payment Flow
  >> 5.4 Agreement Fee Flow
  >> 5.5 Wallet & Credits System
  >> 6. Tenant receives digital receipt (PDF, auto-generated)
  >> 7. Owner receives payment notification (SMS + WhatsApp + in-app)
  >> 8. System logs: payer, payee, amount, property, date, reference
  >> 9. Monthly reminder auto-scheduled (customizable date)
  >> 10. Late payment flag after 5 days overdue
  >> 1. User selects plan
  >> 2. Total breakup shown: Plan fee + GST (18%) + Platform fee (0%)
  >> 3. Payment method selection
  >> 4. UPI: QR or UPI ID (instant, zero cost for platform)
  >> 5. Card: Razorpay checkout (PCI DSS compliant, data stored at Razorpay)
  >> 6. On success: Plan activated instantly
  >> 7. Invoice auto-generated (GST compliant, with HSN code)
  >> 8. Renewal reminder: Day 7, Day 3, Day 1 before expiry
  >> 9. Auto-renewal: Optional (with explicit consent — DPDP compliant)
  >> 1. User selects agreement type (rental / land lease)
  >> 2. System calculates: Stamp duty + FarmerConnect fee + e-stamping fee
  >> 3. Full fee breakdown shown before confirmation
  >> 4. Payment → triggers agreement drafting workflow
  >> 5. Agreement ops executes within 2 hours (Mon–Sat)
  >> 6. Digital agreement delivered to both parties
  >> 7. Physical delivery option: Speed Post (optional, ₹299 extra)
  >> FarmerConnect Credits (FC Credits):
  >> - 1 FC Credit = ₹1 purchasing power within platform
  >> - Earned via: referrals (₹200/successful referral), reviews, milestones
  >> - Used for: contact unlocks (₹9/contact), boost listings, premium search filters
  >> - Expiry: 365 days from earning
  >> - Non-withdrawable (not real money)
  >> - GST not applicable on credit usage (pre-taxed at purchase)

  >> 6.2 Land Verification Process
  >> 6.3 Land Lease Agreement Generation
  >> 6.4 Crop Price Integration
  >> Additional checks for land listings (beyond residential):
  >> 1. Survey number validation (AP/TS land records API integration)
  >> 2. Encumbrance Certificate (EC) check (automated via AP Registration API)
  >> 3. Patta/ROR cross-verification
  >> 4. Pending litigation check (court records API, best-effort)
  >> 5. Land measurement validation (satellite image area estimation via MapBox)
  >> 6. Owner name match: Aadhaar → Patta (same name)
  >> Verification Badge Levels:
  >> - Bronze: Phone + Aadhaar verified
  >> - Silver: + Document verified (Patta + EC)
  >> - Gold: + Physical inspection by FC field agent (Phase 2)
  >> Template: Customizable by state (AP/Telangana/Karnataka specific templates)
  >> Parties: Owner (lessor) + Lessee (tenant farmer)
  >> Content:
  >> - Survey number, area, village, district
  >> - Lease period, start date, end date
  >> - Annual/seasonal lease amount
  >> - Payment schedule (pre-harvest / post-harvest / quarterly)
  >> - Water rights specification
  >> - Crop restriction clauses (if any)
  >> - Renewal terms
  >> - Dispute resolution: Lok Adalat / Arbitration
  >> E-stamp: AP/TS stamp paper (via eStamp portal integration)
  >> E-sign: Aadhaar-based e-sign (DigiLocker / NSDL eSigning)
  >> Delivery: PDF + registered post (optional)
  >> Source: Agmarknet API (Government of India, free)
  >> Display: Current MSP (Minimum Support Price) for crops
  >> Use case: Lessee sees current crop prices → makes informed leasing decision
  >> Alert: Owner notified if nearby market price rises (lease renegotiation signal)
  >> Module 7: PG / Co-Living Module

  >> 1. Seeker finds PG → views photos, reviews, amenities
  >> 2. "Check Availability" → real-time bed status
  >> 3. Schedule visit → owner/caretaker confirms time slot
  >> 4. Visit confirmation: QR code to show at gate
  >> 5. Post-visit: Offer to book → pay ₹1,000 token (refundable if cancelled 48h
  >> before move-in)
  >> 6. Move-in: Photo documentation (checklist: room condition, furniture inventory)
  >> 7. Monthly rent auto-reminder set
  >> 8. Review request sent after 30 days
  >> Module 8: Society Management Module
  >> 8.1 Society Admin Onboarding
  >> 8.2 Society Features
  >> Maintenance Billing & Collection:
  >> Visitor Management:
  >> Community Noticeboard:
  >> Maintenance Requests:
  >> 1. Admin creates society profile (name, address, RWA registration, unit count)
  >> 2. Verification: RWA registration document + admin election proof
  >> 3. Invite residents: Upload CSV of flat numbers + owner names → auto-generate
  >> invite links
  >> 4. Resident app setup: Resident claims their flat via OTP-verified invite
  >> - Admin sets maintenance amount per unit (or per sqft)
  >> - Auto-invoice generated on 1st of each month
  >> - Resident receives bill via app + WhatsApp
  >> - Payment options: UPI, card, netbanking
  >> - Real-time collection dashboard for admin
  >> - Penalty: Auto-calculated for late payments (configurable %)
  >> - Defaulter report: Downloadable CSV
  >> - Bank account: Society's registered account (after penny-drop verification)
  >> - Resident pre-approves visitor via app (generates QR code)
  >> - Guard scans QR at gate → instant approve
  >> - Unannounced visitor: Guard enters name → resident notified → 1-tap approve/deny
  >> - Delivery: One-tap delivery approval (DHL, Amazon, Zomato templates)
  >> - Cab entry: Auto-approve via OTP-linked cab number
  >> - Visitor log: Searchable, 180-day retention
  >> - Admin posts notices (PDF or text)
  >> - Residents post buy/sell/borrow requests
  >> - Emergency alerts: Broadcast with push + SMS
  >> - Polls: Admin creates → residents vote → results public
  >> - Events: Create event → RSVP → reminder
  >> Service Partners (Revenue):
  >> Module 9: Support, Ticketing & RM Dashboard
  >> 9.1 Support Ticket System
  >> - Resident raises ticket (category: plumbing, electrical, lift, common area)
  >> - Photo attachment
  >> - Assigned to maintenance staff by admin
  >> - Status: Open → Assigned → In Progress → Resolved → Rated
  >> - SLA tracking: Admin sees overdue tickets
  >> - Vendor management: Add trusted vendors to society panel
  >> - Society recommends: Housekeeping, tiffin, water cans, pest control
  >> - Vendor listed in app: "Society-approved vendors"
  >> - Resident orders from partner → FarmerConnect earns 8% commission
  >> - Vendor performance: Rated by residents
  >> Channels:
  >> - In-app chat (Chatwoot, self-hosted on Railway free tier)
  >> - WhatsApp Business API (incoming messages routed to Chatwoot)
  >> - Email (support@farmerconnect.in → Chatwoot)
  >> Ticket Categories:
  >> - Listing issue (fake, wrong info, scam concern)
  >> - Payment issue (failed, not credited, refund)
  >> - Agreement issue (delay, error)
  >> - Account issue (login, KYC, plan activation)
  >> - Deal dispute (security deposit, property condition)
  >> - Other
  >> SLA:
  >> - L1 (Support): 4 hours (Mon–Sat), 24 hours (Sun)
  >> - L2 (RM/Finance): 24 hours
  >> - L3 (Legal/Compliance): 72 hours
  >> Auto-resolution:
  >> - Duplicate tickets: Auto-merged
  >> - Known issues: Auto-response with solution
  >> - Payment confirmation queries: Auto-resolved via Razorpay webhook
  >> 9.2 RM Dashboard
  >> SECTION 7 — USER JOURNEYS — STEP-BY-STEP SCREEN
  >> FLOWS
  >> Journey 1: Tenant Finds and Rents a Property
  >> RM sees:
  >> - Assigned tenants (Relax plan holders)
  >> - Tenant preference card (location, budget, BHK, move-in date)
  >> - Shortlisted properties (by system + manually curated)
  >> - Scheduled visits (calendar view)
  >> - Deal status: Open / Visiting / Negotiating / Closed / Lost
  >> RM actions:
  >> - Add property to tenant shortlist
  >> - Schedule visit (owner + tenant notified)
  >> - Mark visit complete + add notes
  >> - Initiate deal confirmation
  >> - Request agreement from agreement ops
  >> - Mark deal "closed" (triggers payout/commission report)
  >> RM performance KPIs:
  >> - Closures per month
  >> - Avg. time to close (days)
  >> - NPS score from assigned tenants
  >> - Tenant plan renewal rate
  >> [DISCOVERY PHASE]
  >> Screen 1: Home → "I'm Looking for a Property" CTA
  >> Screen 2: Search bar + voice input + "Near Me" quick filter
  >> Screen 3: Results grid (10 cards per load, infinite scroll)
  >> Each card: photo, BHK, rent, locality, verified badge, AI match %
  >> Screen 4: Map view toggle → properties shown as pins
  >> Screen 5: Open listing → full gallery, all details, AI summary ("Perfect for 2
  >> working professionals")
  >> [SHORTLISTING PHASE]
  >> Screen 6: Heart icon = shortlist (saved to profile)
  >> Screen 7: Compare mode: Side-by-side 2 properties
  >> Journey 2: Owner Posts a Listing
  >> Screen 8: "Share" → WhatsApp share with property card
  >> [CONTACT PHASE]
  >> Screen 9: "Contact Owner" → Plan check → if free plan: "Upgrade for unlimited" or
  >> "Use 1 credit"
  >> Screen 10: Chat initiated → pre-filled: "Hi, I'm interested in [property]. Is it
  >> available?"
  >> Screen 11: Call option (number-masked WebRTC call)
  >> Screen 12: Schedule visit → date picker → time slot → confirmation
  >> [DEAL PHASE]
  >> Screen 13: Visit completed → tenant marks "Interested"
  >> Screen 14: "Proceed to Agreement" → enter terms (rent, deposit, move-in date)
  >> Screen 15: Agreement form auto-filled → review → e-sign (Aadhaar OTP)
  >> Screen 16: Pay stamp duty + agreement fee
  >> Screen 17: Agreement generated → both parties receive PDF
  >> Screen 18: Set up rent payment → auto-reminder configured
  >> Screen 19: Deal marked "Confirmed" → both parties get confirmation notification
  >> [POST-MOVE PHASE]
  >> Screen 20: Rate owner and property (post 7 days)
  >> Screen 21: Monthly rent payment reminder → one-tap pay
  >> Screen 22: Support channel for any issues
  >> Screen 1: "Post Property" CTA (authenticated user)
  >> Screen 2: Property type selection (grid of icons)
  >> Screen 3: Map → drop pin to mark location → address auto-filled
  >> Screen 4: Basic details form (BHK, floor, area, facing)
  >> Screen 5: Photo upload → guidance overlay ("Take a bright, well-framed photo")
  >> Screen 6: Amenities checklist (50 items with icons, multi-select)
  >> Screen 7: Rent input → AI benchmark shown: "Similar properties: ₹18,000–₹22,000"
  >> Screen 8: Tenant preferences (family/bachelor/any)
  >> Screen 9: Preview full listing
  >> Screen 10: Publish → verification queue → "Under Review (Est. 2 hours)"
  >> Screen 11: Notification: "Listing Live!" → share link
  >> Screen 12: Owner dashboard: Views, contacts, messages
  >> Screen 13: Lead management: Interested seekers list
  >> Screen 14: Visit scheduler: Accept/decline visit requests
  >> Screen 15: Deal confirmation: Mark as "Rented"
  >> Journey 3: Farmer Lists Agricultural Land
  >> Journey 4: PG Seeker Finds and Books PG
  >> Journey 5: Rent Payment Flow
  >> Screen 1: Home → "I'm a Farmer/Land Owner" → "List My Land"
  >> Screen 2: Land type selection (Agricultural / Orchard / Vacant / Mixed)
  >> Screen 3: Survey number + District/Mandal/Village cascading
  >> Screen 4: Area input + unit (acres / cents / guntas — regional units)
  >> Screen 5: Document upload (Patta, ROR) → OCR auto-fills details
  >> Screen 6: Water source, soil type, current crop, suitable crops
  >> Screen 7: Transaction type: Lease (with duration) or Sale
  >> Screen 8: Price input → per acre per year (lease) or per acre (sale)
  >> Screen 9: Land photos (aerial view recommended via drone or satellite capture)
  >> Screen 10: Verification queue → Land records API cross-check
  >> Screen 11: Listing live → shared on WhatsApp communities (integration)
  >> Screen 12: Lease agreement generation (if deal confirmed)
  >> Screen 1: "Looking for PG" → Select gender, location, budget
  >> Screen 2: PG results with photos, star rating, price, distance to college
  >> Screen 3: Open PG listing → photos gallery, room types, meal plan, rules, reviews
  >> Screen 4: Real-time availability: "3 Single rooms available"
  >> Screen 5: "Book a Visit" → instant time slot selection
  >> Screen 6: Visit confirmation QR code generated
  >> Screen 7: Visit → caretaker scans QR → check-in logged
  >> Screen 8: Post-visit: "Book This Room" → pay ₹1,000 token
  >> Screen 9: Move-in checklist: Photo-based room condition documentation
  >> Screen 10: Monthly payment configured → reminder on specified date
  >> Screen 11: Community features: Meet other residents, share concerns
  >> Screen 1: "Pay Rent" → select saved property or add new
  >> Screen 2: Enter amount → purpose: "Rent - January 2025"
  >> Screen 3: Enter owner's UPI ID / bank account (verified)
  >> Screen 4: Payment options: UPI (₹0 fee) / Card (2% fee shown)
  >> Screen 5: Confirm → UPI app opens for payment
  >> Screen 6: Success → receipt generated (PDF, downloadable)
  >> Screen 7: Owner receives notification + PDF receipt
  >> Screen 8: Rent history: All payments with dates, amounts, receipts
  >> Screen 9: Auto-reminder configured for next month
  >> SECTION 8 — DEAL CONFIRMATION & TRANSACTION LOGIC
  >> 8.1 Deal Confirmation Events (Trigger Matrix)
  >> Event 	Confidence
  >> Action
  >> Rental agreement signed via FC platform 	100% 	Auto-mark deal confirmed
  >> First rent paid via FC platform (same
  >> property/owner)
  >> 95% 	Auto-mark deal confirmed
  >> RM manually confirms (Relax plan) 	90% 	Mark confirmed after both parties'
  >> verbal OK
  >> Owner marks listing "Rented" 	70% 	Tentative confirmation, ask tenant to
  >> confirm
  >> Tenant marks listing "Taken" 	70% 	Tentative confirmation, ask owner to
  >> Both parties confirm (mutual) 	100% 	Confirmed
  >> 8.2 Deal Record Schema
  >> 8.3 Impact of Deal Confirmation
  >> "dealId": "FC-DEAL-2024-10892",
  >> "dealType": "rental",
  >> "tenantId": "user_abc123",
  >> "ownerId": "user_xyz789",
  >> "rmId": "rm_001",
  >> "confirmedAt": "2024-01-25T14:00:00Z",
  >> "confirmationMethod": "agreement_signed",
  >> "rentAmount": 25000,
  >> "depositAmount": 75000,
  >> "leaseStartDate": "2024-02-01",
  >> "leaseEndDate": "2025-01-31",
  >> "leaseDurationMonths": 12,
  >> "paymentChannel": "upi",
  >> "agreementId": "AGR-2024-00981",
  >> "propertyCity": "Bengaluru",
  >> "propertyLocality": "Whitefield",
  >> "dealRevenue": {
  >> "agreementFee": 1499,
  >> "subscriptionRevenue": 1499,
  >> "rentPayMDR": 375
  >> "status": "confirmed",
  >> "disputeFlag": false
  >> On Metrics:
  >> - Conversion rate updated (views → contacts → visits → deal)
  >> - RM performance updated
  >> - Listing auto-deactivated (or marked "Rented - Waiting for next availability")
  >> On Incentives:
  >> - RM commission calculated and queued for payout
  >> - Tenant referral credit awarded (if referred)
  >> - Owner loyalty points credited
  >> On Reporting:
  >> - Deal logged in revenue dashboard
  >> SECTION 9 — TECHNICAL ARCHITECTURE — ZERO-INR STACK
  >> 9.1 Architecture Philosophy
  >> "Serverless-first. Pay only for traffic. Scale to billions. Cost: ₹0 until ₹10 Cr revenue."
  >> The entire platform is built on free-tier and usage-based services where fixed costs are ₹0:
  >> 9.2 Zero-INR Infrastructure Stack
  >> Layer 	Service 	Free Tier 	Paid Trigger
  >> Frontend 	Next.js 14 on Vercel 	100GB bandwidth/month 	>100GB
  >> Mobile 	React Native (Expo) 	Build free 	Play Store: $25 one-
  >> time
  >> Backend API 	Supabase Edge
  >> Functions
  >> 2M invocations/month 	>2M
  >> Database
  >> (Primary)
  >> Supabase PostgreSQL 	500MB storage, 2GB
  >> bandwidth
  >> >500MB
  >> Database (Scale) 	PlanetScale (MySQL) 	5GB, 1B row reads 	>5GB
  >> Auth 	Supabase Auth 	Unlimited 	—
  >> Realtime (Chat) 	Supabase Realtime 	Unlimited connections 	—
  >> File Storage 	Cloudflare R2 	10GB storage, 0 egress 	>10GB ($0.015/GB)
  >> CDN 	Cloudflare Free 	Unlimited CDN 	—
  >> Image Processing Cloudflare Images 	100K transforms/month 	>100K
  >> Video 	Cloudflare Stream 	1000 min/month 	>1000 min
  >> Email 	Resend 	3,000 emails/month 	>3,000 ($20/mo)
  >> SMS 	MSG91 / Fast2SMS 	Pay-per-SMS (~₹0.08/SMS) 	Per use
  >> - City/locality deal heat map updated
  >> - Avg. days-to-close metric updated
  >> WhatsApp 	Meta Business API 	1,000 conversations/month
  >> free
  >> >1,000
  >> Maps 	MapBox 	50,000 loads/month 	>50,000
  >> Search (Vector) 	Supabase pgvector 	Included 	—
  >> Full-text Search 	Supabase FTS 	Included 	—
  >> Cache/Queue 	Upstash Redis 	10,000 commands/day 	>10K
  >> Background Jobs 	Trigger.dev 	50,000 runs/month 	>50,000
  >> Monitoring 	Sentry Free 	5,000 errors/month 	>5,000
  >> Analytics 	PostHog Cloud 	1M events/month 	>1M
  >> Logging 	Logflare (Supabase) 	5M logs/month 	>5M
  >> CI/CD 	GitHub Actions 	2,000 min/month 	>2,000
  >> Payments 	Razorpay 	0 fixed, 2%/transaction 	Per transaction
  >> KYC 	DigiLocker API 	Free (government) 	—
  >> E-sign 	NSDL eSigning 	Per sign (~₹15) 	Per use
  >> Calls 	Agora 	10,000 min/month free 	>10,000 min
  >> Total fixed monthly cost: ₹0 Variable cost model: Only pay when revenue flows in
  >> 9.3 System Architecture Diagram (Description)
  >> ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
  >> │ 	CLIENT LAYER 	│
  >> │ Next.js Web App 	React Native Mobile App 	│
  >> │ (Vercel CDN) 	(iOS + Android via Expo) 	│
  >> └─────────────────────────────────────┬───────────────────┘
  >> │ HTTPS/WSS
  >> ┌─────────────────────────────────────▼───────────────────┐
  >> │ 	CLOUDFLARE EDGE (CDN + WAF + DDoS) 	│
  >> │ 	Rate Limiting · Bot Protection · SSL 	│
  >> 9.4 Database Architecture
  >> PostgreSQL Schema (Supabase)
  >> │ 	API GATEWAY LAYER 	│
  >> │ 	Supabase Edge Functions (Deno Runtime) 	│
  >> │ 	Auth Middleware · Rate Limiter · Logger 	│
  >> └──────────┬──────────────┬────────────────────┬──────────┘
  >> │ 	│ 	│
  >> ┌──────────▼──┐ 	┌──────▼───────┐ 	┌──────▼──────────┐
  >> │ CORE DB 	│ 	│ REALTIME 	│ 	│ AI/ML LAYER 	│
  >> │ Supabase │ 	│ Supabase 	│ 	│ OpenAI API 	│
  >> │ PostgreSQL │ 	│ WebSocket │ 	│ (Pay-per-use) │
  >> │ + pgvector │ 	│ (Chat,Push) │ 	│ Embeddings 	│
  >> │ + PostGIS │ 	└──────────────┘ 	│ Recommendations│
  >> └─────────────┘ 	└─────────────────┘
  >> ┌──────────▼──────────────────────────────────────────────┐
  >> │ 	STORAGE & MEDIA LAYER 	│
  >> │ Cloudflare R2 (files) · CF Images · CF Stream (video) │
  >> └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
  >> │ 	BACKGROUND JOBS 	│
  >> │ Trigger.dev · Upstash QStash · Cron (Supabase) 	│
  >> │ - Listing expiry checks 	│
  >> │ - Payment reminders 	│
  >> │ - AI match score computation 	│
  >> │ - Notification dispatch 	│
  >> -- USERS TABLE
  >> CREATE TABLE users (
  >> id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  >> phone VARCHAR(13) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
  >> email VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE,
  >> name VARCHAR(100),
  >> role user_role NOT NULL DEFAULT 'seeker',
  >> kyc_status kyc_status_enum DEFAULT 'unverified',
  >> kyc_level INTEGER DEFAULT 0, -- 0=none, 1=phone, 2=aadhaar, 3=document
  >> aadhaar_hash VARCHAR(64), -- SHA-256 of masked Aadhaar (not stored raw)
  >> pan_hash VARCHAR(64),
  >> profile_photo_url TEXT,
  >> city VARCHAR(100),
  >> preferred_language language_enum DEFAULT 'english',
  >> is_verified BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
  >> is_blocked BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
  >> rera_number VARCHAR(50),
  >> created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  >> updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  >> last_active_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
  >> fcm_token TEXT, -- Firebase push token
  >> metadata JSONB DEFAULT '{}'
  >> -- LISTINGS TABLE
  >> CREATE TABLE listings (
  >> listing_code VARCHAR(30) UNIQUE NOT NULL, -- FC-2024-BLR-10234
  >> owner_id UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  >> property_type property_type_enum NOT NULL,
  >> transaction_type transaction_type_enum NOT NULL,
  >> status listing_status_enum DEFAULT 'draft',
  >> title VARCHAR(200) NOT NULL,
  >> description TEXT,
  >> -- Location
  >> address TEXT,
  >> locality VARCHAR(100),
  >> city VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
  >> state VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
  >> pincode VARCHAR(6),
  >> latitude DECIMAL(10,8),
  >> longitude DECIMAL(11,8),
  >> geo_point GEOGRAPHY(POINT,4326), -- PostGIS
  >> -- Residential fields
  >> bhk INTEGER,
  >> total_area_sqft INTEGER,
  >> carpet_area_sqft INTEGER,
  >> floor INTEGER,
  >> total_floors INTEGER,
  >> furnishing furnishing_enum,
  >> facing facing_enum,
  >> age_years INTEGER,
  >> -- Pricing
  >> rent_monthly INTEGER,
  >> deposit_amount INTEGER,
  >> maintenance_monthly INTEGER,
  >> -- Status
  >> available_from DATE,
  >> is_negotiable BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
  >> -- Agricultural fields
  >> land_area_acres DECIMAL(10,3),
  >> survey_number VARCHAR(50),
  >> land_type land_type_enum,
  >> soil_type soil_type_enum[],
  >> water_source water_source_enum[],
  >> lease_term_years INTEGER,
  >> lease_price_per_acre_year INTEGER,
  >> patta_number VARCHAR(50),
  >> -- Metadata
  >> photos TEXT[],
  >> video_url TEXT,
  >> virtual_tour_url TEXT,
  >> amenities TEXT[],
  >> preferences JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
  >> ai_match_vector vector(1536), -- pgvector embedding
  >> completeness_score INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  >> is_premium BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
  >> verification_notes TEXT,
  >> verified_by UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  >> verified_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
  >> view_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  >> contact_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  >> shortlist_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  >> expires_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
  >> updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
  >> -- DEALS TABLE
  >> CREATE TABLE deals (
  >> deal_code VARCHAR(30) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
  >> listing_id UUID REFERENCES listings(id),
  >> tenant_id UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  >> rm_id UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  >> deal_type deal_type_enum NOT NULL,
  >> status deal_status_enum DEFAULT 'initiated',
  >> confirmation_method deal_confirmation_method_enum,
  >> rent_amount INTEGER,
  >> lease_start_date DATE,
  >> lease_end_date DATE,
  >> agreement_id UUID REFERENCES agreements(id),
  >> confirmed_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
  >> revenue_snapshot JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
  >> dispute_flag BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
  >> notes TEXT,
  >> created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
  >> -- MESSAGES TABLE
  >> CREATE TABLE messages (
  >> conversation_id UUID NOT NULL,
  >> sender_id UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  >> receiver_id UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  >> message_type message_type_enum DEFAULT 'text',
  >> content TEXT,
  >> media_url TEXT,
  >> is_read BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
  >> is_deleted_by_sender BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
  >> -- PAYMENTS TABLE
  >> CREATE TABLE payments (
  >> payment_code VARCHAR(30) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
  >> payer_id UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  >> payee_id UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  >> payment_type payment_type_enum NOT NULL,
  >> amount INTEGER NOT NULL, -- in paise
  >> currency VARCHAR(3) DEFAULT 'INR',
  >> status payment_status_enum DEFAULT 'initiated',
  >> gateway VARCHAR(20),
  >> gateway_order_id VARCHAR(100),
  >> gateway_payment_id VARCHAR(100),
  >> gateway_signature VARCHAR(255),
  >> upi_transaction_id VARCHAR(100),
  >> deal_id UUID REFERENCES deals(id),
  >> plan_id UUID REFERENCES subscription_plans(id),
  >> receipt_url TEXT,
  >> metadata JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
  >> -- SUBSCRIPTIONS TABLE
  >> CREATE TABLE subscriptions (
  >> user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  >> plan_code VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
  >> plan_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
  >> user_role user_role NOT NULL,
  >> status sub_status_enum DEFAULT 'active',
  >> amount_paid INTEGER NOT NULL,
  >> starts_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,
  >> expires_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,
  >> payment_id UUID REFERENCES payments(id),
  >> rm_assigned UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  >> auto_renew BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
  >> -- AGREEMENTS TABLE
  >> CREATE TABLE agreements (
  >> agreement_code VARCHAR(30) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
  >> agreement_type agreement_type_enum NOT NULL,
  >> status agreement_status_enum DEFAULT 'draft',
  >> stamp_duty INTEGER,
  >> fc_fee INTEGER,
  >> total_paid INTEGER,
  >> document_url TEXT,
  >> signed_document_url TEXT,
  >> tenant_signed_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
  >> owner_signed_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
  >> delivery_address TEXT,
  >> physical_delivery_opted BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
  >> dispatched_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
  >> tracking_number VARCHAR(50),
  >> content JSONB NOT NULL, -- Full agreement terms
  >> -- REVIEWS TABLE
  >> CREATE TABLE reviews (
  >> reviewer_id UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  >> reviewee_id UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  >> review_type review_type_enum NOT NULL,
  >> overall_rating DECIMAL(2,1) CHECK (overall_rating BETWEEN 1 AND 5),
  >> dimensions JSONB DEFAULT '{}', -- {cleanliness: 4.5, owner_behavior: 5, value: 4}
  >> comment TEXT,
  >> is_verified_deal BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
  >> upvotes INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  >> is_published BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
  >> -- SUPPORT TICKETS TABLE
  >> CREATE TABLE support_tickets (
  >> ticket_code VARCHAR(20) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
  >> category ticket_category_enum NOT NULL,
  >> priority ticket_priority_enum DEFAULT 'medium',
  >> status ticket_status_enum DEFAULT 'open',
  >> 9.5 API Design
  >> Base URL Structure
  >> Authentication
  >> Core API Endpoints
  >> subject VARCHAR(200),
  >> attachments TEXT[],
  >> assigned_to UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  >> sla_deadline TIMESTAMPTZ,
  >> resolved_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
  >> resolution_notes TEXT,
  >> satisfaction_rating INTEGER CHECK (satisfaction_rating BETWEEN 1 AND 5),
  >> Production: https://api.farmerconnect.in/v1
  >> Staging: 	https://api-staging.farmerconnect.in/v1
  >> Type: JWT Bearer Token (Supabase Auth)
  >> Header: Authorization: Bearer <supabase_jwt>
  >> Refresh: /auth/refresh
  >> Token expiry: 1 hour (access), 30 days (refresh)
  >> yaml
  >> # AUTH
  >> POST /auth/otp/send 	# Send OTP to phone
  >> POST /auth/otp/verify 	# Verify OTP → returns JWT
  >> POST /auth/refresh 	# Refresh access token
  >> DELETE /auth/session 	# Logout
  >> # USERS
  >> GET 	/users/me 	# Get current user profile
  >> PATCH /users/me 	# Update profile
  >> POST /users/kyc/initiate 	# Start KYC process
  >> GET 	/users/kyc/status 	# Get KYC status
  >> POST /users/kyc/upload 	# Upload KYC documents
  >> # LISTINGS
  >> GET 	/listings 	# Search listings (params: q, type, city, lat, lng, r
  >> POST /listings 	# Create listing
  >> GET 	/listings/:id 	# Get listing detail
  >> PATCH /listings/:id 	# Update listing
  >> DELETE /listings/:id 	# Delete listing
  >> POST /listings/:id/photos 	# Upload photos
  >> GET 	/listings/:id/contacts # Get contact requests for this listing
  >> POST /listings/:id/shortlist # Shortlist a listing
  >> DELETE /listings/:id/shortlist # Remove from shortlist
  >> POST /listings/:id/report 	# Report a listing
  >> GET 	/listings/my 	# Get my listings (owner)
  >> PATCH /listings/:id/status 	# Update status (active/paused/rented)
  >> # SEARCH
  >> GET 	/search/listings 	# Full-text + vector search
  >> GET 	/search/suggest 	# Autocomplete suggestions
  >> GET 	/search/nearby 	# Nearby properties (lat, lng, radius)
  >> GET 	/search/agri 	# Agricultural land search
  >> # CONTACTS
  >> POST /contacts 	# Unlock contact (deducts credit or checks plan)
  >> GET 	/contacts/history 	# Contact history
  >> # MESSAGES
  >> GET 	/conversations 	# Get all conversations
  >> POST /conversations 	# Start conversation
  >> GET 	/conversations/:id/messages # Get messages
  >> POST /conversations/:id/messages # Send message
  >> # DEALS

  >> GET 	/deals/:id 	# Get deal details

  >> # ANALYTICS (Internal)
  >> SECTION 10 — SECURITY ARCHITECTURE — BANK-GRADE
  >> 10.1 Security Principles
  >> Zero Trust: Every request re-authenticated, no implicit trust
  >> Defense in Depth: Multiple layers of protection
  >> Privacy by Design: Minimal data collection, maximum encryption
  >> DPDP Act 2023 Compliance: India's data protection framework
  >> 10.2 Authentication & Authorization
  >> 10.3 Data Encryption
  >> GET 	/analytics/listings 	# Listing performance metrics
  >> GET 	/analytics/platform 	# Platform-level metrics (admin)
  >> Multi-Factor Authentication (MFA):
  >> Layer 1: Phone OTP (mandatory for all users)
  >> Layer 2: Aadhaar OTP (for KYC level 2+)
  >> Layer 3: TOTP (Google Authenticator) for internal admins
  >> Session Management:
  >> - JWT with short expiry (1 hour access token)
  >> - Refresh token rotation on each use
  >> - Concurrent session limit: 5 devices
  >> - Force logout: Admin can invalidate all sessions
  >> Row-Level Security (RLS):
  >> - Supabase RLS policies on every table
  >> - Users can only read/write their own data
  >> - Admin bypass via service_role key (backend-only, never exposed to client)
  >> - Example policy:
  >> CREATE POLICY "Users can only see own listings" ON listings
  >> FOR SELECT USING (owner_id = auth.uid() OR status = 'active');
  >> At Rest:
  >> - Supabase: AES-256 encryption at disk level
  >> - Cloudflare R2: Server-side encryption (AES-256)
  >> 10.4 API Security
  >> - Aadhaar numbers: Never stored raw; stored as SHA-256 hash
  >> - PAN numbers: Masked (XXXXX1234F format stored)
  >> - Bank account numbers: Encrypted with AES-256-GCM before storage
  >> - Credit card data: Never stored (Razorpay vaulted)
  >> In Transit:
  >> - TLS 1.3 minimum for all connections
  >> - HSTS header enforced
  >> - Certificate Transparency monitoring
  >> Application Level:
  >> - Chat messages: E2E encrypted (Signal Protocol via libsodium WASM)
  >> - Call recordings: AES-256 at rest, deleted after 90 days
  >> - Payment data: Never logged in application logs
  >> Rate Limiting (Cloudflare + Upstash Redis):
  >> - Auth endpoints: 5 requests/minute per IP
  >> - Search: 60 requests/minute per user
  >> - Contact unlock: 20/day per user (free tier)
  >> - File upload: 100MB/day per user
  >> - OTP send: 5 attempts/10 minutes per phone
  >> Input Validation:
  >> - All inputs validated on server (Zod schema validation)
  >> - SQL injection prevention: Parameterized queries (Supabase client)
  >> - XSS prevention: Content Security Policy headers
  >> - SSRF prevention: Whitelist of allowed external URLs
  >> - File upload: MIME type validation, virus scan (ClamAV on edge function)
  >> Injection Prevention:
  >> - All DB queries via Supabase SDK (never raw SQL from user input)
  >> - Listing descriptions: Sanitized (DOMPurify server-side)
  >> - Phone number regex validation: /^[6-9]\d{9}$/
  >> - Pincode validation: /^\d{6}$/
  >> API Key Management:
  >> - No keys in frontend code (all in Vercel env vars)
  >> - Razorpay: Server-side signature verification on every webhook
  >> - Third-party keys rotated quarterly
  >> - Secrets stored in Supabase Vault (encrypted KV)
  >> 10.5 Fraud Detection
  >> 10.6 Compliance
  >> Listing Fraud Signals:
  >> - Duplicate photo detection (perceptual hash)
  >> - Price anomaly: >40% below market → flag for review
  >> - Phone number in description: Auto-redact + flag
  >> - "Broker" keywords detected: Auto-flag
  >> - New account + immediate listing: Extra verification required
  >> - Multiple listings from same IP (different accounts): Alert
  >> User Fraud Signals:
  >> - Multiple accounts from same Aadhaar hash: Block + alert
  >> - Mass contact unlock (>50/day): Suspicious → rate limit
  >> - Fake review detection: ML model on review text patterns
  >> - Payment fraud: Razorpay fraud detection integrated
  >> Automated Responses:
  >> - Risk score < 30: Auto-block
  >> - Risk score 30–60: Manual review
  >> - Risk score > 60: Auto-approve
  >> - Repeated flags: Account suspension → support ticket for appeal
  >> DPDP Act 2023:
  >> - Privacy policy: Plain language, vernacular versions
  >> - Consent: Explicit, granular, withdrawable
  >> - Data minimization: Only collect what's needed
  >> - Right to erasure: Account deletion API
  >> - Data retention: Defined per data type:
  >> - Active listing data: Retained while active + 6 months
  >> - Deal records: 7 years (legal requirement)
  >> - Chat messages: 90 days after conversation closes
  >> - Call recordings: 90 days
  >> - KYC documents: 5 years (PMLA requirement)
  >> - Payment records: 7 years (Income Tax)
  >> - Marketing data: Until consent withdrawn
  >> IT Act 2000 Compliance:
  >> - E-sign under Section 5 (legal validity)
  >> - Intermediary guidelines (Rule 3(1)(b) content moderation)
  >> - Grievance officer: Named, contact published (mandatory)
  >> SECTION 11 — UI/UX DESIGN SYSTEM
  >> 11.1 Design Philosophy
  >> "Familiar but better" — The design should feel instantly familiar to Indian smartphone users
  >> Core Design Tenets:
  >> Mobile-first (80% of traffic will be mobile)
  >> Vernacular-ready (RTL and Indic script support)
  >> Low-bandwidth friendly (compressed images, skeleton screens)
  >> Accessibility: WCAG 2.1 AA compliant
  >> One-thumb operation on 5.5" screens
  >> 11.2 Design Tokens
  >> - CSAM policy: Zero tolerance, NCMEC reporting
  >> RERA Compliance:
  >> - Broker RERA number mandatory for broker listings
  >> - Agent listings flagged if RERA expired
  >> - State-specific RERA rules applied
  >> RBI Payment Compliance:
  >> - PCI DSS via Razorpay (no card data on FC servers)
  >> - UPI compliance via licensed payment aggregators
  >> - Settlement: T+2 for rent payments (per RBI guidelines)

  >> Principles:
  >> - Duration: 150ms (micro) to 400ms (page transitions)
  >> - Easing: ease-out for entries, ease-in for exits
  >> - Reduce motion: Respect prefers-reduced-motion media query
  >> Key Animations:
  >> - Card enter: Fade up 8px (150ms ease-out)
  >> - Filter apply: Slide in from right (250ms)
  >> - Photo gallery: Native-feel swipe (spring physics)
  >> - Map pins: Scale in with bounce (200ms)
  >> - Deal confirmation: Confetti burst (300ms) + success card
  >> - Loading: Skeleton shimmer (1.5s linear infinite)
  >> - OTP input: Shake on error (300ms ease-out)
  >> - Verified badge: Pulse on first render

  >> 12.1 Platform-Level Metrics (Admin Dashboard)
  >> 12.2 Owner Analytics Dashboard
  >> Real-Time Dashboard:
  >> - Active listings count (by type, city)
  >> - New registrations today
  >> - Searches in last hour

  >> - Revenue by stream (subscriptions, agreements, rent pay, ads)
  >> - City-wise performance
  >> - Plan conversion rates (free → paid)
  >> - Churn rate by plan type
  >> - NPS score trend
  >> - RM performance matrix
  >> Per Listing Metrics:
  >> - Total views (today / week / all time)
  >> - Unique visitors
  >> - Shortlist count
  >> - Contact unlocks (who contacted: verified/unverified)
  >> - Call connections count
  >> - Visit schedules
  >> - Conversion funnel: Views → Contacts → Visits → Deal
  >> Listing Quality Score:
  >> - Photo quality: /25
  >> - Details completeness: /25
  >> - Response rate: /25
  >> - Review score: /25
  >> - Total: /100 → displayed as "Property Score"
  >> Insights:
  >> 12.3 AI Intelligence Layer
  >> - "Your listing gets 3x more views with 360° tour"
  >> - "Properties with >8 photos get 60% more contacts"
  >> - "Optimal rent for your locality: ₹22,000–₹25,000"
  >> Feature 1: Smart Matching Engine
  >> Input: Seeker preference profile (stated + behavioral)
  >> Output: Ranked listing recommendations
  >> Algorithm: Collaborative filtering + content-based hybrid
  >> Vector: pgvector cosine similarity on listing embeddings
  >> Update frequency: Real-time on new listings + daily batch rerank
  >> Feature 2: Fair Rent Predictor
  >> Input: City, Locality, BHK, area, furnishing, amenities
  >> Output: Fair rent range (min, median, max)
  >> Model: Gradient boost on historical deals + active listings
  >> Displayed: On listing creation for owners + on listing for seekers
  >> Feature 3: Fraud Scorer
  >> Input: User behavior, listing attributes, device signals
  >> Output: Risk score (0–100)
  >> Triggers: New listing, first contact, payment attempt
  >> Action: Auto-approve / Review / Block
  >> Feature 4: AI Listing Summary
  >> Input: Listing details + photos
  >> Output: 2-sentence human-readable summary ("Perfect for working couples —
  >> spacious east-facing flat with parking, 5 mins from metro.")
  >> Model: GPT-4o-mini (pay-per-use, ~₹0.002/listing)
  >> Feature 5: Vernacular Voice Search
  >> Input: Voice in Telugu/Hindi/Kannada
  >> Output: Structured search query
  >> Model: OpenAI Whisper (free self-host) → intent extraction → search API
  >> Feature 6: Deal Probability Predictor
  >> Input: Contact history, visit count, days on market, seeker profile
  >> Output: Deal probability % (shown to RM)
  >> Action: RM prioritizes high-probability cases

  >> Mobile TTI (Time to Interactive) 	< 3.5s 	Lighthouse

  >> - payment.captured → activate subscription / confirm payment
  >> - payment.failed → notify user + retry prompt
  >> - refund.created → notify user

  >> - document_fetched → trigger KYC processing

  >> Listing creation to live 	< 2 hours 	Internal SLA
  >> 14.2 Scalability Design
  >> 14.3 Availability & Reliability
  >> Horizontal Scaling:
  >> - Supabase: Auto-scales (managed)
  >> - Vercel: CDN auto-scales globally
  >> - Cloudflare: 200+ PoPs globally
  >> - Edge Functions: Serverless = infinite horizontal scale
  >> Database Scaling:
  >> - Connection pooling: Supabase PgBouncer
  >> - Read replicas: Enabled at scale ($25/month — only when needed)
  >> - Caching strategy:
  >> - Hot listings cached in Upstash Redis (5 min TTL)
  >> - Search results cached by query hash (2 min TTL)
  >> - User profile cached (10 min TTL)
  >> - Database indexes:
  >> - listings: (city, status, property_type, rent_monthly, geo_point GIST)
  >> - listings: full-text tsvector index
  >> - listings: pgvector IVFFLAT index for AI search
  >> - messages: (conversation_id, created_at)
  >> - payments: (payer_id, created_at)
  >> Traffic Estimation:
  >> - Yr 1: 10K DAU → Supabase free handles comfortably
  >> - Yr 2: 1L DAU → Supabase Pro ($25/month)
  >> - Yr 3: 10L DAU → Supabase Team + read replica ($200/month)
  >> - Yr 5: 1Cr DAU → Supabase Enterprise (negotiated)
  >> Uptime SLA Target: 99.9% (8.7 hours downtime/year)
  >> Dependency SLAs (provider guarantees):
  >> - Supabase: 99.9%
  >> - Vercel: 99.99%
  >> - Cloudflare: 99.99%
  >> SECTION 15 — COMPLIANCE, LEGAL & KYC FRAMEWORK
  >> 15.1 KYC Levels & Access Rights
  >> Level 	Verification 	Access Granted
  >> 0 — Unverified 	None 	Browse only
  >> 1 — Phone Verified 	Phone OTP 	Browse + shortlist + 3 contacts
  >> 2 — Identity Verified 	Phone + Aadhaar 	All seeker features
  >> 3 — Document Verified 	+ Ownership docs / Patta 	Create listings
  >> 4 — Premium Verified 	+ Video KYC 	Verified badge, higher trust score
  >> 15.2 Data Retention Schedule
  >> Data Type 	Retention 	Reason
  >> Active user data 	While account active 	Service delivery
  >> Deleted account data 	30 days (then anonymized) 	DPDP erasure right
  >> KYC documents 	5 years from last transaction 	PMLA compliance
  >> Payment records 	7 years 	Income Tax Act
  >> - Razorpay: 99.99%
  >> Failure Handling:
  >> - Circuit breaker: Auto-fallback if AI service down (skip AI, show basic
  >> results)
  >> - Payment fallback: If Razorpay down → switch to Cashfree
  >> - Offline mode: PWA service worker caches last search results
  >> - Graceful degradation: Core search + view works without auth
  >> Backup Strategy:
  >> - Supabase: Daily automated backups (PITR 7 days on Pro)
  >> - Cloudflare R2: Versioned storage
  >> - Configuration: Infrastructure as Code (Terraform) in GitHub
  >> Deal records 	7 years 	Legal evidence
  >> Chat messages 	90 days post-closure 	Dispute resolution
  >> Call recordings 	90 days 	Dispute resolution
  >> Listing data 	90 days post-expiry 	Analytics
  >> Server logs 	30 days 	Security
  >> 15.3 User Rights (DPDP Act 2023)
  >> Right 	Implementation
  >> Right to access 	"Download my data" in settings → JSON export
  >> Right to correction 	Edit profile, re-submit KYC
  >> Right to erasure 	"Delete my account" → 30-day grace → purge
  >> Right to portability 	Data export includes all listings, deals, messages
  >> Right to grievance 	Grievance officer contact in app footer
  >> Right to nominate 	Nominee can access account on death
  >> 15.4 Grievance Officer (Mandatory under IT Rules)
  >> Name: [Company-designated officer]
  >> Contact: grievance@farmerconnect.in
  >> Phone: [Support number]
  >> Address: [Registered office]
  >> Response SLA: 48 hours (mandatory under Rule 3(1)(b))
  >> Resolution SLA: 30 days

  >> - Mobile: Expo React Native
  >> Requirements:
  >> - OTP sent to Indian phone numbers only (regex: /^[6-9]\d{9}$/)
  >> - Rate limit: 5 OTP attempts per 10 minutes per phone
  >> - JWT stored in httpOnly cookie (web) / SecureStore (mobile)
  >> - Auto-refresh before expiry
  >> - Multi-device session management
  >> - Logout from all devices option

  >> Prompt 2: Listing Search Module
  >> Prompt 3: Real-Time Chat Module
  >> Build a high-performance property search system using:
  >> - Supabase PostgreSQL (PostGIS for geospatial, pgvector for AI search, tsvector
  >> for full-text)
  >> - Next.js 14 API routes (Supabase Edge Functions)
  >> - TypeScript
  >> - Text search on: title, description, locality, city, amenities
  >> - Filter support: 25+ filters (BHK, rent range, furnishing, property type, etc.)
  >> - Geospatial: radius search (ST_DWithin) from user lat/lng
  >> - AI semantic search: pgvector cosine similarity on listing embeddings
  >> - Sorting: relevance, rent (asc/desc), date, AI match score
  >> - Pagination: cursor-based (not offset, for performance)
  >> - Response: paginated listing cards (minimal data for list view)
  >> - Caching: Upstash Redis (2-min TTL per unique query hash)
  >> - Performance target: p95 < 500ms
  >> - Database indexes (optimized for this query pattern)
  >> - Search API endpoint with full filter support
  >> - Cursor-based pagination implementation
  >> - Redis caching layer
  >> - Example queries with EXPLAIN ANALYZE results
  >> Build a real-time encrypted chat system using:
  >> - Supabase Realtime (PostgreSQL → WebSocket)
  >> - libsodium (E2E encryption, WASM in browser)
  >> - React (web) + React Native (mobile)
  >> - One-to-one chats (seeker ↔ owner, per listing context)
  >> - E2E encrypted (client-side encrypt before storing)
  >> - Message types: text, photo, quick-reply
  >> - Delivery status: sent → delivered → read
  >> - Typing indicator (ephemeral, not stored)
  >> - Auto-redact phone numbers from message content
  >> - Block/report user

  >> SECTION 18 — RISK REGISTER & EDGE CASE CATALOG
  >> 18.1 Business Risks
  >> Risk 	Probability Impact 	Mitigation
  >> Broker infiltration (fake owner
  >> listings)
  >> High 	High 	KYC + ownership doc verification;
  >> broker-detect AI
  >> Fake listings (scam properties) 	High 	High 	Multi-layer verification; real-time fraud
  >> score
  >> NoBroker legal challenge 	Medium 	Medium Operate differently — agri module is
  >> unique moat; legal counsel
  >> Low conversion (free → paid) 	Medium 	High 	RM-guided free trial; strong feature
  >> gating
  >> Payment failures / UPI downtime 	Low 	Medium Fallback gateway; auto-retry logic
  >> Government data API downtime
  >> (Dharani, DigiLocker)
  >> Medium 	Low 	Cache last known good response; queue
  >> retry
  >> Data breach 	Low 	Very
  >> High
  >> Encryption at rest/transit; penetration
  >> testing; cyber insurance
  >> 18.2 Technical Edge Cases
  >> Edge Case 1: Same Aadhaar on multiple accounts
  >> Detection: Hash Aadhaar; check uniqueness before KYC approval
  >> Action: Block new account; send alert to admin; notify user to merge
  >> Edge Case 2: Owner lists property already rented
  >> Detection: Check for active deals on same listing
  >> Action: Warn owner; auto-suspend after confirmation of old deal
  >> Edge Case 3: Seeker pays rent to wrong person
  >> Detection: Bank validation before first payment; review period
  >> Action: Support ticket escalation; coordinate refund via Razorpay
  >> Edge Case 4: Agreement signed but deal falls through
  >> Detection: Both parties mark "deal cancelled" within 7 days
  >> Action: Agreement voided (legal note); partial refund of FC fee
  >> 18.3 Society Edge Cases
  >> Edge Case 5: Agricultural land with disputed title
  >> Detection: Litigation check via court records API (best-effort)
  >> Action: "Dispute check pending" badge; warn lessee before deal
  >> Edge Case 6: PG closes down mid-stay
  >> Detection: Multiple resident complaints; owner not responding
  >> Action: Residents get priority listings access; refund of advance
  >> Edge Case 7: Society admin account hacked
  >> Detection: Login from new device + bulk action triggered
  >> Action: Auto-suspend bulk action; OTP re-verification; alert
  >> Edge Case 8: Chat message with bank account request
  >> Detection: Regex + ML model detects banking credential request
  >> Action: Message hidden + warning shown; flag for review
  >> Edge Case 9: Listing photos from stock image site
  >> Detection: Reverse image search (Google Vision API or perceptual hash)
  >> Action: Reject listing; ask for original photos with timestamp
  >> Edge Case 10: User uploads Aadhaar with edited details
  >> Detection: OCR + DigiLocker cross-check; document metadata analysis
  >> Action: KYC rejected; account flagged; notify Aadhaar authority if pattern
  >> detected
  >> Edge Case 1: Multiple admins conflict
  >> Resolution: Super-admin role hierarchy; majority vote for major decisions
  >> Edge Case 2: Resident disputes maintenance charge
  >> Resolution: Appeal to society committee; support ticket to FC
  >> Edge Case 3: Owner of unit not resident (rented out)
  >> Resolution: Both owner + tenant can be registered; owner approves tenant profile
  >> Edge Case 4: Society RWA disputes FC's management role
  >> Resolution: Clear ToS: FC is tool, not managing committee; data exportable

FARMERCONNECT PLATFORM
Complete Product Requirements Document — Billion-Dollar Edition
Version 1.0 | Confidential & Proprietary
Architecture: Zero-INR Infrastructure · Serverless-First · Globally Scalable
Vision Statement: Build the most trusted, inclusive, and intelligent property + agricultural
land platform in India — eliminating brokers, reducing friction, and connecting every
property type (urban residential, rural agricultural, commercial, PG/co-living) directly
between owners and seekers — powered by AI, secured at bank grade, and operated at zero
infrastructure cost.

SECTION 1 — EXECUTIVE SUMMARY
1.1 Product Identity
Field 	Detail
Product Name 	FarmerConnect
Tagline 	Every Property. Every Acre. Zero Broker.
Category 	PropTech + AgriTech Marketplace
Geography 	India (Phase 1: Tier 1-2 cities + rural Andhra Pradesh, Telangana, Karnataka)
Target TAM 	₹4,50,000 Cr+ Indian real estate + ₹12,000 Cr agri-land market
Launch Target 	10,000 listings · 50,000 users in first 90 days
Infrastructure Cost 	₹0/month (zero-INR serverless stack)
Maintenance Model Self-healing, auto-scaling, event-driven
1.2 The Problem We Solve
India's property market is deeply broken across five dimensions:
1. Urban Renters pay 1–2 months' brokerage (₹10,000–₹60,000) for every house move —
often every 11 months due to short lease cycles.
2. Agricultural Landowners have NO digital platform to list, lease, or sell farm land — relying
entirely on local middlemen who charge 3–5% commissions.
3. Rural Migrants moving to cities for work have zero trusted platform to find affordable PG
or shared accommodation in safe localities.
4. Property Owners (NRI & Local) struggle to find verified tenants and manage rent
collection, agreements, and maintenance remotely.
5. Society Admins have fragmented tools for visitor management, complaint tracking,
payments collection, and community communication.
1.3 The FarmerConnect Solution
A unified, AI-first, zero-broker property marketplace that serves:
Urban rental seekers
Agricultural land seekers and owners
PG/co-living seekers
Society communities
Property managers and NRI landlords
What makes it a ₹1,000 Cr+ platform:
Uniquely covers agricultural + urban properties (no competitor does both)
Zero-broker direct connect with AI-powered matching
Built on ₹0/month infrastructure (Supabase + Cloudflare + Vercel)
Bank-grade security without enterprise cost
Vernacular-first (Telugu, Kannada, Hindi, Tamil alongside English)

Housing.com 	✅ 	❌ 	❌ 	❌ 	❌ 	❌
Zolo/Stanza 	❌ 	❌ 	✅ 	❌ 	✅ 	❌
MyGate 	❌ 	❌ 	❌ 	✅ 	N/A 	❌
FarmerConnect ✅ 	✅ 	✅ 	✅ 	✅ 	✅
FarmerConnect is the ONLY platform covering all six dimensions simultaneously.
2.3 Unique Differentiators (Moat Builders)
1. Agricultural Land Module — First-ever structured digital marketplace for farm land
(lease, sale, joint farming arrangements)
2. Vernacular-First Interface — Full Telugu, Kannada, Hindi support with voice search
3. Offline-Capable PWA — Works in low-connectivity rural areas via service workers
4. AI Matchmaker — Proprietary scoring engine that matches properties to seekers based on
stated + inferred preferences
5. Zero Broker Guarantee — Platform-level mechanism that detects and penalizes broker
infiltration
6. Instant Digital Agreement — E-sign rental + land lease agreements in under 10 minutes
7. Transparent Price Intelligence — AI-predicted fair market rent based on locality, BHK,
season, and supply-demand
SECTION 3 — PRODUCT VISION, MISSION & PRINCIPLES
3.1 Vision
"To democratize property access for every Indian — from a farm worker in Nellore to a
software engineer in Bengaluru — through trust, transparency, and technology."
3.2 Mission
Build a platform so trustworthy and simple that a farmer in rural Andhra Pradesh can list his 5-
acre land for lease with the same confidence as a Bengaluru techie finding a 2BHK — in their
own language, from their own phone.
3.3 Core Design Principles
Principle 	Meaning in Practice
Trust First 	Every user, listing, and transaction is verified before going live
Zero Friction 	Any key action (search, contact, pay) completes in ≤3 taps
Privacy by Default 	Phone numbers never exposed; calls go through masked numbers
Vernacular Native 	No user should be disadvantaged by their language
Offline Resilient 	Core search and viewing works without internet
Transparent Pricing 	No hidden fees; all charges shown upfront before confirmation
Data Sovereignty 	User data never sold; DPDP Act 2023 compliant by design

  >> 3.2 Microservice Boundaries & Responsibilities
  >> 3.2.1 API Gateway
  >> The API Gateway is the single ingress point for all client traffic. It handles:
  >> JWT validation and token refresh before forwarding requests to downstream services
  >> Rate limiting per user per endpoint (configurable per plan tier)
  >> Request/response transformation for versioned APIs
  >> SSL termination and DDoS protection via Cloudflare
  >> Logging of every request with correlation IDs for distributed tracing
  >> A/B testing header injection for experiment routing
  >> 3.2.2 User Management Service
  >> Owns the users, user_locations, seller_profiles, buyer_profiles, and verification_documents tables
  >> Issues signed JWTs (RS256) with role claims (buyer, seller, admin, support)
  >> Handles OTP-based phone number authentication via SMS (primary) and WhatsApp (fallback)
  >> Manages KYC document upload, storage, and status tracking
  >> Exposes a gRPC endpoint for other services to validate tokens without round-tripping to the gateway
  >> 3.2.3 Marketplace Services (Crop / Equipment / Services / Jobs)
  >> Each service owns its own PostgreSQL schema on Supabase
  >> Communicates with User Service via gRPC for seller/buyer profile lookups
  >> Publishes domain events (ListingCreated, OrderPlaced, BookingConfirmed) to the Kafka event bus
  >> Maintains its own search index via webhook pushes to the Search Service on create/update/delete
  >> 3.2.4 Unified Payment & Financial Services Cluster
  >> 3.3 Event-Driven Communication
  >> Event Name
  >> Producer
  >> Consumers
  >> Payload Key Fields
  >> user.registered
  >> Notification, Analytics
  >> user_id, phone, language
  >> listing.created
  >> Any Marketplace
  >> Search Service, Analytics
  >> listing_id, type, seller_id, location

  >> 3.4 Infrastructure-as-Code (Zero INR Bootstrap Strategy)
  >> Zero-Cost Stack Summary
  >> Migration Triggers: Upgrade to paid tiers when any of the following thresholds are crossed:
  >> Database storage exceeds 400MB on Supabase → migrate to dedicated Supabase Pro ($25/month)
  >> MAU exceeds 40,000 → upgrade Supabase Auth tier
  >> Railway service memory exceeds 512MB consistently → upgrade to Starter plan ($5/month/service)
  >> Cloudflare Workers requests exceed 80K/day → upgrade to Workers Paid ($5/month, 10M req)
  >> 4. Complete Database Schema
  >> 4.1 Design Principles
  >> UUID primary keys everywhere — prevents enumeration attacks and enables distributed ID generation
  >> Every table has created_at and updated_at timestamps with automatic triggers
  >> Soft deletes using deleted_at nullable timestamp — no hard deletes on business data
  >> JSONB for flexible metadata — never create a column for data that varies per record type
  >> 4.2 Core User Management Schema
  >> Table: users
  >> Column
  >> Type
  >> Constraints
  >> Description
  >> UUID
  >> PK, Default: gen_random_uuid()
  >> Unique user identifier
  >> phone_number
  >> VARCHAR(20)
  >> UNIQUE, NOT NULL, CHECK (phone_number ~ '^\+[1-9]\d{6,14}$')
  >> E.164 format phone — primary identity
  >> password_hash
  >> VARCHAR(255)
  >> NOT NULL
  >> Argon2id hashed password
  >> full_name
  >> VARCHAR(100)
  >> Display name
  >> profile_picture_url
  >> VARCHAR(500)
  >> NULLABLE
  >> CDN URL to profile image
  >> preferred_language
  >> VARCHAR(10)
  >> NOT NULL, DEFAULT 'hi'
  >> BCP-47 language code (hi, te, ta...)

  >> BOOLEAN
  >> NOT NULL, DEFAULT false
  >> OTP verification completed
  >> kyc_status
  >> kyc_status_enum
  >> NOT NULL, DEFAULT 'none'

  >> 5. Security Architecture
  >> Security Philosophy
  >> 5.1 Authentication & Authorization
  >> 5.1.1 Authentication Stack
  >> 5.1.2 Authorization Model — Role-Based Access Control (RBAC)
  >> Role
  >> Scope
  >> Key Permissions
  >> buyer
  >> Own data only
  >> Browse listings, place orders, view own orders, manage own profile, initiate disputes on own orders
  >> seller
  >> Own listings/orders
  >> employer
  >> Own job posts
  >> Create/edit job postings, view applicants for own jobs, contact applicants
  >> job_seeker
  >> Own applications
  >> Browse jobs, apply, track own applications, update resume profile
  >> support
  >> Read-only most data
  >> View user profiles, orders, disputes — cannot modify financial records
  >> admin
  >> Full platform
  >> super_admin
  >> Full platform + infra
  >> All admin permissions plus payment gateway config, platform fee changes, data export
  >> Row-Level Security (RLS) Policies — All Supabase tables enforce RLS. Example policies:
  >> RLS Policy Example
  >> 5.2 Data Security
  >> 5.2.1 Encryption Standards
  >> Data Type
  >> Encryption Standard
  >> Implementation
  >> Passwords
  >> Argon2id
  >> Memory: 64MB, Iterations: 3, Parallelism: 4
  >> Data at Rest (DB)
  >> AES-256-GCM
  >> Supabase/PostgreSQL encrypted volumes
  >> Data in Transit
  >> TLS 1.3
  >> Enforced at Cloudflare edge, HSTS headers, no TLS 1.0/1.1
  >> PII Fields (Aadhaar)
  >> AES-256 + application-level
  >> Field-level encryption on sensitive KYC data before DB storage
  >> Bank Account Numbers
  >> AES-256 + tokenization
  >> Only last 4 digits stored in DB; full number via Razorpay tokenization
  >> API Keys / Secrets
  >> HashiCorp Vault / Doppler
  >> Never hardcoded; injected as environment variables at runtime
  >> Backup Data
  >> AES-256
  >> Encrypted before upload to cold storage
  >> Media Files (CDN)
  >> Signed URLs
  >> All private documents accessed via time-limited signed URLs (15 min TTL)
  >> 5.3 API Security
  >> 5.4 Fraud Detection & Prevention
  >> 5.4.1 Real-Time Fraud Signals
  >> Signal
  >> Detection Method
  >> Automated Action
  >> Multiple accounts same phone
  >> Phone number uniqueness + device fingerprint
  >> Block registration, flag for review
  >> Abnormal listing price
  >> Statistical deviation from market price (±3σ)
  >> Hold listing for admin review before publishing
  >> Rapid bulk listing creation
  >> Rate limiting + velocity check (>10 listings/hour)
  >> Temporary account suspension + CAPTCHA
  >> Payment amount mismatch
  >> Server-side amount verification before gateway call
  >> Reject payment, log security event
  >> Geo velocity anomaly
  >> Login location changes faster than physically possible
  >> Force re-authentication + security alert to user
  >> Fake review attempt
  >> Reviewer must have completed transaction with reviewee
  >> Review submission blocked if no verified transaction
  >> Escrow manipulation
  >> Status transitions validated against allowed state machine
  >> Reject invalid transitions, alert security team
  >> Collusive transactions
  >> Graph analysis: same device, IP, or bank account on both buyer/seller
  >> Flag for manual review, hold payouts

  >> 6.2 Backend Performance Optimizations
  >> 6.2.1 Database Query Optimization
  >> PostGIS spatial indexes (GIST) on all geography columns for sub-50ms radius queries
  >> Cursor-based pagination on all list endpoints — no OFFSET pagination on large tables
  >> 6.2.2 Caching Strategy
  >> Cache Layer
  >> Invalidation Strategy
  >> Active listing data
  >> 5 minutes
  >> Event-driven: invalidate on listing update/delete
  >> User profile data
  >> In-process memory (LRU)
  >> 2 minutes
  >> Invalidate on profile update event
  >> Category lists
  >> 24 hours
  >> Manual flush on admin category change
  >> Market price data
  >> 1 hour
  >> Scheduled refresh from external APIs
  >> Search results
  >> Meilisearch internal cache
  >> 30 seconds
  >> Auto-invalidated on index update
  >> Crop price predictions
  >> 6 hours
  >> ML model deployment triggers invalidation
  >> Static app config
  >> CDN Edge Cache
  >> 7 days
  >> Cache-busting via content hash in URL
  >> Seller stats (dashboard)
  >> 15 minutes
  >> Scheduled recalculation via cron
  >> 6.3 Mobile Performance Optimizations
  >> FlatList / LazyColumn with keyExtractor and getItemLayout for 60fps scrolling on long listing lists
  >> React.memo / useMemo aggressive memoization on all list item components
  >> Hermes JavaScript engine (React Native) — reduces JS bundle parse time by ~60% on low-end devices
  >> Proguard/R8 code shrinking on Android release builds — reduces DEX size by ~30%

  >> 7.3 Voice Input System
  >> Voice input is not an optional feature — it is a primary input method. Implementation requirements:
  >> Voice input button (microphone icon) present on every text input field in the app
  >> Language auto-detected from user's preferred_language setting, with manual override
  >> Real-time transcription displayed as user speaks (streaming ASR via Google Speech-to-Text API)
  >> Confirmation UI: User sees transcribed text before form submission, with easy tap-to-edit
  >> Voice search: Holding the main search bar microphone icon activates voice search mode

  >> 7.5.1 Local Database Schema (SQLite on Device)
  >> Local Table
  >> Data Stored
  >> Sync Direction
  >> Eviction Policy
  >> local_listings_cache
  >> Last 200 viewed/searched listings with full data
  >> Server → Client
  >> LRU eviction, max 200 entries
  >> local_draft_listings
  >> Unsent listing creations by this seller
  >> Client → Server (on sync)
  >> Delete after successful server sync
  >> local_draft_orders
  >> Unsent order placement attempts
  >> Delete after server confirms or user cancels
  >> local_messages_cache
  >> Last 50 messages per active conversation
  >> Bidirectional
  >> Keep 7 days, then evict
  >> local_price_cache
  >> Last-fetched price predictions per crop + location
  >> Expire after 6 hours
  >> local_profile_cache
  >> Own user/seller profile data
  >> sync_queue
  >> Pending write operations awaiting connectivity
  >> Client → Server (on reconnect)
  >> Retry up to 10 times, then surface to user
  >> local_categories
  >> All category data for all 4 marketplaces
  >> Expire after 24 hours

  >> 8. Marketplace Feature Specifications
  >> 8.1 Crop Marketplace — Full Feature Specification
  >> 8.1.1 Seller: Creating a Crop Listing (Step-by-Step Flow)
  >> 8.1.2 Buyer: Search & Discovery Flow
  >> Smart Filters (always visible as horizontal chip row below search):
  >> Proximity: 10km / 25km / 50km / 100km / State / Country — powered by PostGIS radius query
  >> Category: Multi-select chip selector
  >> Price: Range slider with min/max in local unit
  >> Quality: Grade A / Organic / Premium checkboxes
  >> Availability: Available now / Within 7 days / Within 30 days
  >> Verified Sellers Only: Toggle
  >> Sort Options: Nearest first (default) / Lowest price / Highest rated / Newest listings
  >> 8.2 Equipment Rental Marketplace — Full Feature Specification
  >> 8.2.1 Availability Calendar System
  >> Real-time availability calendar is a core feature. Implementation:
  >> Calendar stored as a set of "blocked" date ranges in the equipment_availability_blocks table
  >> On the renter-facing booking screen, unavailable dates are shown in grey and non-tappable
  >> When a booking is confirmed, the booked dates are automatically added to the blocked ranges
  >> 8.2.2 GPS Tracking for High-Value Equipment
  >> During an active rental, both provider and renter can view real-time location on an in-app map
  >> Location data is deleted 48 hours after rental completion (privacy compliance)
  >> 8.3 Rural Services Marketplace — Full Feature Specification
  >> 8.3.1 Service Booking & Appointment Flow
  >> 8.4 Rural Job Marketplace — Full Feature Specification
  >> 8.4.1 Job Seeker Profile Builder
  >> Multi-step profile builder designed for users with no formal resume experience:
  >> Step 1 — Personal info: Name, location, preferred work radius
  >> Step 3 — Skills: Tag-based selector. 200+ pre-defined rural skills. Voice-add custom skills
  >> Step 5 — Wage expectation: Per-day slider with market rate guidance shown
  >> Step 7 — Profile photo: Required for trust. Camera integration with face-detection crop guide
  >> 8.4.2 One-Tap Apply
  >> The entire job application flow must complete in < 3 taps from the job listing screen:
  >> Tap 1: "Apply Now" button on job listing
  >> Tap 2: Review pre-filled application (profile data auto-populated), optional cover note via voice
  >> Tap 3: "Submit Application" — done
  >> 9. Escrow System — Complete State Machine
  >> 9.1 State Machine Definition
  >> State
  >> Meaning
  >> Who Can Trigger Transition From This State
  >> Possible Next States
  >> AWAITING_PAYMENT
  >> Order created, payment not yet received
  >> Buyer (pay) / System (auto-cancel after 30 min)
  >> FUNDED, CANCELLED
  >> FUNDED
  >> Payment received and held in escrow
  >> Seller (mark shipped/started) / Buyer (cancel within window)
  >> SHIPPED, IN_PROGRESS, CANCELLATION_REQUESTED
  >> SHIPPED
  >> Goods dispatched (Crop marketplace)
  >> Buyer (confirm received) / System (auto-accept after 72h) / Buyer (reject)
  >> DELIVERED, REJECTED
  >> IN_PROGRESS
  >> Service underway (Services marketplace)
  >> Provider (mark completed) / Buyer (raise issue)
  >> COMPLETED_PENDING, DISPUTED
  >> DELIVERED
  >> Buyer confirmed receipt of goods
  >> Buyer (accept / reject within inspection window)
  >> ACCEPTED, REJECTED
  >> COMPLETED_PENDING
  >> Provider marked service complete
  >> Buyer (confirm / raise issue within 48h)
  >> ACCEPTED, DISPUTED
  >> ACCEPTED
  >> Buyer confirmed satisfaction
  >> System (auto-trigger fund release)
  >> RELEASING_FUNDS
  >> Commission calculated, payout initiated
  >> System (payout success/failure)
  >> COMPLETED, PAYOUT_FAILED
  >> COMPLETED
  >> Final state — funds released to seller
  >> N/A (terminal state)
  >> REJECTED
  >> Buyer rejected goods within inspection window
  >> System (start 72h negotiation period)
  >> IN_DISPUTE, REFUNDED (if seller agrees)
  >> IN_DISPUTE
  >> Formal dispute filed, funds frozen
  >> Arbitrator (decide outcome)
  >> REFUNDED, PARTIALLY_REFUNDED, COMPLETED
  >> REFUNDED
  >> Full refund issued to buyer
  >> PARTIALLY_REFUNDED
  >> Split decision by arbitrator
  >> CANCELLED
  >> Order cancelled before funding
  >> PAYOUT_FAILED
  >> Payout to seller failed (bank error)
  >> Finance team (retry) / System (auto-retry x3)
  >> COMPLETED, MANUAL_REVIEW

  >> 10. AI & Machine Learning Integration
  >> 10.1 Crop Price Prediction — Technical Architecture
  >> 10.1.1 Data Pipeline
  >> The prediction engine is fed by a multi-source data pipeline ingesting five categories of data:
  >> Data Source
  >> Ingestion Method
  >> Update Frequency
  >> Fields Used
  >> Agmarknet / UPAg (India)
  >> Government market prices
  >> REST API + daily scraper fallback
  >> Daily
  >> commodity, market, min_price, max_price, modal_price, date
  >> IMD Weather API
  >> Weather forecasts
  >> REST API
  >> Every 6 hours
  >> temperature, rainfall, humidity, district
  >> NASA MODIS NDVI
  >> Satellite vegetation index
  >> GeoTIFF download + processing
  >> Every 8 days
  >> NDVI value per pixel, date, bounding box
  >> Kisan Connect user data
  >> Crowdsourced prices
  >> Internal event stream
  >> Real-time
  >> crop, reported_price, location, date, user_reputation
  >> Festival / holiday calendar
  >> Demand shock events
  >> Static + annual update
  >> Annual
  >> festival_name, date, affected_commodities, historical_demand_multiplier
  >> 10.1.2 Feature Engineering
  >> Lag features: price(t-1), price(t-7), price(t-14), price(t-30) per commodity per market
  >> Rolling statistics: 7-day mean, 7-day std dev, 30-day mean (captures seasonal volatility)
  >> Weather features: 7-day forecast avg temperature, total rainfall forecast, humidity index
  >> NDVI delta: Change in vegetation index from previous period (leading indicator of yield)
  >> Festival proximity: Days to nearest high-demand festival, with commodity-specific demand weight
  >> Price momentum: Rolling 7-day price change percentage (captures trending markets)
  >> Market connectivity: Distance from production region to nearest APMC market (affects price spread)

  >> 11.1 Gateway Abstraction Layer

  >> 11.2 Gateway Selection & Routing
  >> Payment Method
  >> Primary Gateway
  >> Fallback Gateway
  >> Routing Rationale
  >> UPI (any app)
  >> PhonePe Payment Gateway
  >> Razorpay
  >> PhonePe has highest UPI success rates in rural India
  >> UPI Collect (intent)
  >> Cashfree
  >> Razorpay has better SDK coverage for intent flow
  >> UPI AutoPay (subscriptions)
  >> Razorpay UPI AutoPay has widest bank support
  >> Bank Transfer / NEFT
  >> Standard NEFT support
  >> Debit Card
  >> Paytm
  >> Razorpay card success rates and 3DS support
  >> Net Banking
  >> Standard implementation
  >> Wallet (Paytm/Amazon Pay)
  >> Razorpay aggregates major wallets
  >> USSD (*99#)
  >> Direct NPCI integration
  >> Feature phone support — no internet required

  >> Processing Fee

  >> 14.1 Commission Structure by Marketplace
  >> Commission Type
  >> Rate (Free Tier)
  >> Rate (Standard)

  >> 14.2 Unit Economics Model (Year 1 Target)
  >> Target (EOY1)
  >> Assumptions
  >> Monthly Active Users (MAU)
  >> 50,000
  >> Hyper-local + 5-district expansion phase
  >> Active Sellers/Providers
  >> 5,000
  >> 10% of MAU in seller mode
  >> Monthly Transactions
  >> 15,000
  >> 3 transactions/active seller/month avg
  >> Average Transaction Value
  >> ₹1,800
  >> Blended across all 4 marketplaces
  >> Gross Merchandise Value (GMV)
  >> ₹2.7 Cr/month
  >> Transactions × Avg Transaction Value
  >> Blended Commission Rate
  >> Mix of marketplace types and seller tiers
  >> Gross Revenue
  >> ₹16.2 L/month
  >> GMV × Commission Rate
  >> Subscription MRR
  >> ₹3 L/month
  >> 1,500 paid sellers × ₹200 avg plan
  >> Featured Listings & One-Time
  >> ₹1.5 L/month
  >> Estimated from listing volume
  >> Total MRR
  >> ₹20.7 L/month
  >> Sum of all revenue streams
  >> Infrastructure Cost (Zero-Cost Strategy)
  >> ₹0 (free tiers)
  >> Scales to ₹1–2L/month at 50K MAU if needed
  >> Customer Acquisition Cost (CAC)
  >> ₹150–200 per user
  >> Kisan Mitra commissions + digital marketing
  >> Lifetime Value (LTV) — Seller
  >> ₹12,000–18,000
  >> Based on 24-month retention × avg monthly commission
  >> LTV/CAC Ratio
  >> >10x
  >> Healthy for SaaS-style marketplace
  >> 15. DevOps, CI/CD & Infrastructure
  >> 15.1 CI/CD Pipeline
  >> Stage
  >> Trigger
  >> Action
  >> Gate
  >> Code Push
  >> GitHub / GitLab
  >> Every push to any branch
  >> Pre-commit hooks: lint, format, type-check
  >> Block push if lint fails
  >> Pull Request
  >> GitHub Actions
  >> PR opened/updated
  >> Run unit tests, integration tests, contract tests, SAST scan, bundle size check
  >> All checks must pass before merge
  >> Merge to Staging
  >> Merge to staging branch
  >> E2E tests pass, no regressions
  >> Production Deploy
  >> Manual trigger OR merge to main
  >> Blue-green deploy to production, smoke tests, automated rollback if error rate > 2% in 5 minutes
  >> Manual approval required + automated health check
  >> Mobile Build
  >> EAS Build (Expo)
  >> Git tag with version (v1.x.x)
  >> QA sign-off required for store submission
  >> 15.2 Monitoring & Observability Stack
  >> 15.3 Disaster Recovery
  >> Component
  >> RTO (Recovery Time)
  >> RPO (Data Loss Tolerance)
  >> Strategy
  >> Database (Supabase)
  >> < 1 hour
  >> < 5 minutes
  >> Supabase automated daily backups + WAL point-in-time recovery (paid tier)
  >> Application Services (Railway)
  >> < 10 minutes
  >> Zero (stateless)
  >> Railway auto-redeploy from last successful build on health check failure
  >> Media Storage (Cloudflare R2)
  >> Near-zero
  >> R2 built-in multi-region replication
  >> Message Queue (Upstash Kafka)
  >> < 1 minute
  >> Upstash multi-zone replication
  >> Cache (Upstash Redis)
  >> < 2 minutes
  >> Acceptable (cache is cold-startable)
  >> Redis RDB snapshots + auto-recovery on restart
  >> DNS / Edge (Cloudflare)
  >> Cloudflare anycast network; automatic failover

  >> 19.1 Core API Conventions
  >> Base URL: https://api.kisanconnect.in/v1
  >> Authentication: Bearer {JWT} header on all authenticated endpoints
  >> Content-Type: application/json on all requests and responses
  >> Pagination: Cursor-based. Response includes {data: [], cursor: "opaque_string", has_more: bool}
  >> Success format: {success: true, data: {...}, meta: {request_id, timestamp}}
  >> Rate limit headers: X-RateLimit-Limit, X-RateLimit-Remaining, X-RateLimit-Reset on every response

Table of Contents
1. Executive Summary
Kisan Connect is a unified rural super-app designed to digitize and democratize the rural economy of India and eventually emerging markets across Asia and Africa. The platform integrates four high-frequency, high-trust marketplaces — Crop Trading, Equipment Rental, Rural Services, and Rural Employment — into a single, dual-mode application that serves both Buyers/Service Seekers and Sellers/Service Providers.
This Product Requirements Document (PRD) is the single authoritative source of truth for the design, engineering, and go-to-market execution of Kisan Connect. It is written to be handed directly to a cross-functional developer team and AI pair-programming assistants as a complete, actionable blueprint requiring zero follow-up documents.
Vision Statement
To become the indispensable digital infrastructure for 500 million rural citizens, enabling every farmer, artisan, tradesperson, and household to participate fully and fairly in the digital economy — regardless of connectivity, device, or digital literacy level.
1.1 The Opportunity
India's rural economy accounts for nearly 46% of national income yet remains severely underserved by digital platforms. Farmers lose up to 30% of post-harvest value due to information asymmetry and middlemen. Equipment idle time costs billions annually. Service providers lack discovery mechanisms. Rural youth face structural unemployment despite growing skill levels. Kisan Connect addresses all four pain points through a single platform with a unified identity layer, shared payment rails, and a trust engine powered by escrow, reviews, and AI verification.
1.2 Core Differentiators
Offline-First Architecture: Full functionality in 2G/no-connectivity environments via local SQLite caching and background sync queues
Escrow-as-Standard: Every transaction — crop, equipment, service — is protected by a mandatory escrow engine with a structured dispute resolution state machine
AI Price Intelligence: Proprietary LSTM-based crop price prediction model trained on government APIs, satellite imagery, weather feeds, and crowdsourced farmer data
Dual-Mode UX: A single app switches seamlessly between Buyer and Seller mode, reducing fragmentation and increasing platform stickiness
Zero-Infrastructure Cost Bootstrap: Designed to run on free-tier cloud infrastructure (Supabase, Railway, Vercel, Cloudflare Workers) during MVP phase with a clear migration path to production-grade cloud
Regional Language First: Full UI/UX in 12 Indian languages with voice-input and text-to-speech at every input point
